# Galactic Republic

[Edit](/wiki/Galactic_Republic?veaction=edit) 

* [Edit source](/wiki/Galactic_Republic?action=edit)
* [History](/wiki/Galactic_Republic?action=history)
* [Purge](/wiki/Galactic_Republic?action=purge)
* [Talk (53)](/wiki/Talk:Galactic_Republic)

[![This article details a subject that is considered canon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/Canon "This article details a subject that is considered canon.")

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [This article covers the Canon version of this subject.](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "This article covers the Canon version of this subject.") |  | [Click here for Wookieepedia's article on the Legends version of this subject.](/wiki/Galactic_Republic/Legends "Click here for Wookieepedia's article on the Legends version of this subject.") |  |

[![OnACanonArticle](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/Canon "Canon")[![GoToLegends](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/Galactic_Republic/Legends "Galactic Republic/Legends")

This article is about **the Galactic Republic, also referred to as the "Old Republic."** You may be looking for **the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"), which was formed by the [Rebel Alliance](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic")**.

For other uses, see **[The Old Republic](/wiki/The_Old_Republic_(disambiguation) "The Old Republic (disambiguation)")**.

## Historical information

### Date established

c.[25,000 BBY](/wiki/25,000_BBY "25,000 BBY")[[12]](#cite_note-Altdate_and_Restoration_date-12)[[13]](#cite_note-Falcon_26-13) —c. [20,000 BBY](/wiki/20,000_BBY "20,000 BBY")[[14]](#cite_note-Timelines-14)

19 BBY[[15]](#cite_note-Galactic_Atlas-15)

### Date restored

* [1032 BBY](/wiki/1032_BBY "1032 BBY"),[[12]](#cite_note-Altdate_and_Restoration_date-12) as the modern Galactic Republic[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Government)

:   "*The Galactic Republic was the Republic of legend, greater than distance or time.*"
:   ―Janyor[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

The **Galactic Republic**, also known as the **Grand Republic** or simply as the **Republic**, was a [democratic](/wiki/Democracy "Democracy") [federal union](/wiki/Politics#Republic "Politics") spread across [light-years](/wiki/Light-year "Light-year") of [space](/wiki/Realspace "Realspace"). Due in part to its long history, different names were used for bygone incarnations or eras of the Republic. The **Old Republic** and the **first Galactic Republic** were terms affixed to the original incarnation of the Republic that existed until its [fall](/wiki/Fall_of_the_Old_Republic "Fall of the Old Republic") to the [Sith Empire](/wiki/Sith_Empire "Sith Empire"), which in turn fell in [1032 BBY](/wiki/1032_BBY "1032 BBY"), leading to the restoration of the Republic in that year. Later, the modern Republic that had been supplanted by the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY") was also referred to as the Old Republic. Additionally, the **High Republic** was a term used to describe the modern Republic during the [era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era") in which it had reached the zenith of its power, which lasted from around [500 BBY](/wiki/500_BBY "500 BBY") to around [100 BBY](/wiki/100_BBY "100 BBY").

The Republic was originally founded many [millennia](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium") before the [Battle of Yavin](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin"), approximately around [25,000 BBY](/wiki/25,000_BBY "25,000 BBY") to [20,000 BBY](/wiki/20,000_BBY "20,000 BBY"). The [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate") governed the Republic under the [Galactic Constitution](/wiki/Galactic_Constitution "Galactic Constitution"), and comprised thousands of [senators](/wiki/Senator "Senator") representing the Republic's member worlds. The [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") was the title of the head of the Republic, elected from ranks of the Senate to lead the government on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"). An [ecumenopolis](/wiki/Ecumenopolis "Ecumenopolis") or [city](/wiki/City "City")-covered [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet"), referred to as [Galactic City](/wiki/Imperial_City "Imperial City"), Coruscant was the [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") of the Republic and therefore the [seat of the Senate](/wiki/Imperial_Senate_Building "Imperial Senate Building").

The Galactic Republic and it [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") shared sovereignty, and spanned a multiplicity of worlds from the [Core Worlds](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds") to the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories"), uniting a variety of [sentient](/wiki/Sentience "Sentience") [species](/wiki/Species "Species"), [human](/wiki/Human "Human") and [alien](/wiki/Alien "Alien") alike, under [one banner](/wiki/Republic_crest "Republic crest"). As its power grew, the Republic fought many wars against various opponents such as [Mandalorians](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian"), the [Zygerrian Slave Empire](/wiki/Zygerrian_Slave_Empire "Zygerrian Slave Empire"), the [Nihil](/wiki/Nihil "Nihil"), and several [Sith Empires](/wiki/Sith_Empire "Sith Empire"). The [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") Order, a [religious](/wiki/Religion "Religion") group of [Force-sensitives](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") dedicated to the [light side of the Force](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force "Light side of the Force"), was sworn to the service of the Senate, and as such the [Jedi Knights](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") were hailed as the guardians of peace and justice within the Republic. [Centuries](/wiki/Standard_century "Standard century") of conflict culminated in the [fall of the Old Republic](/wiki/Fall_of_the_Old_Republic "Fall of the Old Republic"), and the [last war](/wiki/Jedi-Sith_War "Jedi-Sith War") between the ancient Jedi and [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") concluded with the restoration and rise of the modern Galactic Republic, ushering in the [Republic Era](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era") which was an age of peace that lasted for a thousand [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year"). The Republic's [history](/wiki/Timeline_of_galactic_history "Timeline of galactic history") was officially reset, and the ages before this event were merged into a collective whole known as the [Old Republic-era](/wiki/Old_Republic-era "Old Republic-era").

The Republic entered a period of decline after centuries of expansion and prosperity. Aided by the [resurgent](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two") [Sith Lords](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord"), the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") divided the galaxy between the Republic [loyalists](/wiki/Loyalist "Loyalist") and the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"). The [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic") was organized under the leadership of [Jedi Generals](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") who led the [Republic Military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military") against the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army") during the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"). However, the conflict had been [orchestrated](/wiki/Grand_Plan "Grand Plan") to allow Supreme Chancellor [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious")—the alter ego of [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious, the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith")—to control and deceive the Republic in a [dictatorial](/wiki/Dictatorship "Dictatorship") manner. With the [end](/wiki/Battle_of_Utapau "Battle of Utapau") of the war, Sidious initiated the [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") through [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66") and transformed the Republic into the Galactic Empire by [declaring](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") himself [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor"). The [Imperial Senate](/wiki/Imperial_Senate "Imperial Senate") stood as the last remnant of the Old Republic until it was [disbanded](/wiki/Dissolution_of_the_Imperial_Senate "Dissolution of the Imperial Senate") by the [Emperor](/wiki/Emperor "Emperor") at the height of the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"). In the aftermath of the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War"), the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") was fully [reorganized](/wiki/Declaration_of_a_New_Republic "Declaration of a New Republic") into the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"), restoring the Galactic Republic after a generation of [Imperial rule](/wiki/Fascism "Fascism").

## History[]

### Birth of freedom[]

:   "*For over a thousand generations the Jedi Knights were the guardians of peace and justice in the Old Republic. Before the dark times. Before the Empire.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi[[19]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-19)

 [![The pre-modern Galactic Republic was referred to as the "Old Republic](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/OldRepublicEmblem.svg/revision/latest?cb=20250720043825) [![The pre-modern Galactic Republic was referred to as the "Old Republic](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/OldRepublicEmblem.svg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20250720043825)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/da/OldRepublicEmblem.svg/revision/latest?cb=20250720043825) 

The pre-modern Galactic Republic was referred to as the "Old Republic."

 

The original [Galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") Republic was formed between approximately [25,000 BBY](/wiki/25,000_BBY "25,000 BBY")[[12]](#cite_note-Altdate_and_Restoration_date-12)[[13]](#cite_note-Falcon_26-13) and [20,000 BBY](/wiki/20,000_BBY "20,000 BBY")[[14]](#cite_note-Timelines-14) and rose to power by expanding across [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy"),[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) with several of its founding members being the [planets](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan")[[20]](#cite_note-HC_1-20) and [Chandrila](/wiki/Chandrila "Chandrila").[[21]](#cite_note-HC_9-21) Around [20,019 BBY](/wiki/20,019_BBY "20,019 BBY"), the [Thisspiasian](/wiki/Thisspiasian "Thisspiasian") [Blood Monarchy](/wiki/Blood_Monarchy "Blood Monarchy") joined the Galactic Republic in its early formation.[[22]](#cite_note-Blood_Court_note-22) Multiple versions of the Republic existed throughout its extensive [history](/wiki/Timeline_of_galactic_history "Timeline of galactic history"); [historians](/wiki/Historian "Historian") referred to this pre-modern period as the "Old Republic,"[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) although the government's official name was the Galactic Republic.[[23]](#cite_note-Chaos_Rising-23) The [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") of the Old Republic was located on an [ecumenopolis](/wiki/Ecumenopolis "Ecumenopolis") known as [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant") and would remain there for thousands of [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year").[[24]](#cite_note-Capital-24)

At one time, Coruscant's fellow [city](/wiki/City "City")-world of [Troithe](/wiki/Troithe "Troithe") rivaled it as the Republic's cosmopolitan center, holding a population in the billions. A notable portion of those citizens belonged to major [merchant](/wiki/Merchant "Merchant") and [noble](/wiki/Noble "Noble") families. However, Coruscant ultimately outpaced Troithe in industrial growth. As years passed, Troithe fell into decline.[[25]](#cite_note-Shadow_Fall-25) At least five [millennia](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium") before the start of the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War"),[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26) a [rogue faction](/wiki/Jedi_splinter_group "Jedi splinter group") of [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") broke away from the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"), believing that practicing the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") would benefit the furthering of Jedi power. This schism divided the Order on ideological grounds, igniting an event known as the [Hundred-Year Darkness](/wiki/Hundred-Year_Darkness "Hundred-Year Darkness"), which, in turn, resulted in the formation of the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith").[[27]](#cite_note-Sith-27) At one point, they managed to construct a [dark shrine](/wiki/Shrine_in_the_Depths "Shrine in the Depths") on Coruscant. The rogue faction was ultimately [defeated](/wiki/Sith_war_(Old_Republic) "Sith war (Old Republic)"), and they were [exiled](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant_(Sith_war) "Battle of Coruscant (Sith war)") from the Old Republic into uncharted [space](/wiki/Realspace "Realspace").[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5)

At some point, the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") was constructed over the Sith shrine in order to contain its dark energy.[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5) Once it had established itself on Coruscant, the Jedi Order closely associated itself with the Old Republic, serving as guardians of the peace and justice for over a thousand generations.[[19]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-19) Little did the Jedi know, the Sith had regrouped on the planet [Moraband](/wiki/Moraband "Moraband").[[27]](#cite_note-Sith-27)

Thousands of years before the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"), the [Corellian royalty](/wiki/Corellian_royalty "Corellian royalty") sponsored exploration and colonization efforts that helped expand the frontiers of the Old Republic.[[28]](#cite_note-Official_Guide-28) [Hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace") travel would prove to be the key to the Republic's expansion beyond the [Core Worlds](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds").[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

### A clash of destinies in the galaxy[]

:   "*The history of the Ascendancy is in these rooms, some of the pieces dating back to Chiss participation in the wars between the Galactic Republic and the Sith Empire.*"
:   ―[Mitth'raw'nuruodo](/wiki/Mitth%27raw%27nuruodo "Mitth'raw'nuruodo"), to [Ar'alani](/wiki/Ar%27alani "Ar'alani")[[23]](#cite_note-Chaos_Rising-23)

As the Old Republic spread its influence across the [stars](/wiki/Star "Star"), it came into contact with various other powers, one of them being the [Zygerrian Slave Empire](/wiki/Zygerrian_Slave_Empire "Zygerrian Slave Empire"). Due to the fact that, at some point in its past, the Old Republic declared [slavery](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery") illegal and expected other civilizations of the galaxy to comply, it took an aggressive stance against the [Zygerrians](/wiki/Zygerrian "Zygerrian"). The Zygerrian Empire, which was built upon slavery, refused to comply, forcing both the Old Republic and the Jedi to intervene. After joining together, the Old Republic and Jedi Order sent their [armies](/wiki/Army "Army") [against](/wiki/Jedi%E2%80%93Zygerrian_conflict "Jedi–Zygerrian conflict") the empire after the Zygerrians refused. The Old Republic ultimately came out victorious, driving the practice of slave trading into the underworld, dismantling the empire, and confining what was left of its government to [Zygerria](/wiki/Zygerria "Zygerria"), the civilization's [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld").[[29]](#cite_note-Zygerrian_Databank-29) Another one was the rogue [Predori](/wiki/Predori "Predori") empire.[[30]](#cite_note-ALD-30)

 [![Destructive wars were fought between the Sith and the Jedi in the age of the Old Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/GreatScourgeofMalachor-TotA1.png/revision/latest?cb=20201027144205) [![Destructive wars were fought between the Sith and the Jedi in the age of the Old Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/GreatScourgeofMalachor-TotA1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201027144205)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/GreatScourgeofMalachor-TotA1.png/revision/latest?cb=20201027144205) 

Destructive wars were fought between the Sith and the Jedi in the age of the Old Republic.

 

Eventually, the Sith would return in full strength, invading the Old Republic. From there, the dark Order would do battle with the Jedi and the Old Republic. This would lead to a series of conflicts between both groups that would go on for thousands of years until the Old Republic's ultimate collapse.[[27]](#cite_note-Sith-27) During one of the wars, the Jedi [fought](/wiki/Great_Scourge_of_Malachor "Great Scourge of Malachor") the [Sith Empire](/wiki/Sith_Empire "Sith Empire") on [Malachor](/wiki/Malachor "Malachor"), which proved to be one of the most devastating battles in the history of the Order.[[31]](#cite_note-Twilight_of_the_Apprentice-31)

At some point, the Old Republic came into contact with the [Mandalorian](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian") people. The warrior civilization began a series of unprovoked military [campaigns](/wiki/Mandalorian_crusades "Mandalorian crusades") against the Old Republic. Later on, after all-out [war](/wiki/Mandalorian-Jedi_War "Mandalorian-Jedi War") erupted, the Jedi stepped in to defend the Republic.[[32]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-32) In the meantime, Republic and Jedi forces continued to wage war against the expanding Sith Empire. During these wars, both sides would construct massive [superweapons](/wiki/Superweapon "Superweapon") powered by large [kyber crystals](/wiki/Kyber_crystal "Kyber crystal") capable of mass destruction.[[33]](#cite_note-The_Big_Bang-33)[[34]](#cite_note-Death_Star_Superlaser-34)

The [Middle Era of the Old Republic](/wiki/Middle_Era_of_the_Old_Republic "Middle Era of the Old Republic") was one period of galactic history.[[35]](#cite_note-Guardians_of_the_Whills-35) The Galactic Republic also participated in the [Sith Wars](/wiki/Sith_Wars "Sith Wars"), a series of conflicts against the Sith Empire and involving the [Chiss Ascendancy](/wiki/Chiss_Ascendancy "Chiss Ascendancy"). The Ascendancy encountered a number of [aliens](/wiki/Alien "Alien") before retreating to their borders.[[23]](#cite_note-Chaos_Rising-23)

### Fall of the Old Republic[]

:   "*This lightsaber was stolen from your Jedi Temple by my ancestors during the fall of the Old Republic.*"
:   ―Pre Vizsla, to Obi-Wan Kenobi, regarding the Darksaber[[32]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-32)

 [![The Mandalorian Wars brought on the beginning of the Old Republic's downfall.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/Mandalore_mural.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250926050127) [![The Mandalorian Wars brought on the beginning of the Old Republic's downfall.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/Mandalore_mural.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250926050127)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/Mandalore_mural.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250926050127) 

The Mandalorian Wars brought on the beginning of the Old Republic's downfall.

 

With the civilization of the Sith and the warrior culture of [Mandalore](/wiki/Mandalore "Mandalore"), and with their beliefs of continual warfare without regard to the Jedi mandate of protecting the weak, the Jedi Order continued to mobilize its forces in an effort to stop enemy incursions into Old Republic space.[[32]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-32)[[27]](#cite_note-Sith-27)

The power of the Sith Empire increased during the [fall of the Old Republic](/wiki/Fall_of_the_Old_Republic "Fall of the Old Republic"). The Sith soon achieved near-dominance across the galaxy.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) It was also during this time that an ancestor of [Pre Vizsla](/wiki/Pre_Vizsla "Pre Vizsla"),[[36]](#cite_note-Rebels_Recon_#3.14-36) leader of the Mandalorian group [Death Watch](/wiki/Death_Watch "Death Watch") during the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), managed to steal the [Darksaber](/wiki/Darksaber "Darksaber") from the Jedi [Temple](/wiki/Jedi_temple "Jedi temple").[[32]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-32)

At some point the galaxy entered a state known as the Dark Age. During this time, the [Jedi-Sith War](/wiki/Jedi-Sith_War "Jedi-Sith War") broke out. Early on in this conflict, the Old Republic capital world of Coruscant was taken over by the Sith during the [Battle of Coruscant](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant_(Jedi-Sith_War) "Battle of Coruscant (Jedi-Sith War)"). Later on in the war, the Sith were driven off the planet by the Jedi during the [Liberation of Coruscant](/wiki/Liberation_of_Coruscant "Liberation of Coruscant").[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

### The fires of hope[]

:   "*The Republic victory was so definitive that it reinvented itself, resettling its capital on Coruscant after a devastating ouster. History reset its chrono on this date, and from that moment, the modern Galactic Republic was born.*"
:   ―Janyor[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

The Old Republic managed to regain some of its strength after its forces had reclaimed the capital, capable of going on the offensive.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) The Jedi were strong enough to finally end its ancient war against the Mandalorian clans. A [battle](/wiki/Annihilation "Annihilation") between both groups on the planet Mandalore left the planet ravaged and lifeless.[[37]](#cite_note-Gauntlet_fighter-37) It was during this time too when the Sith were finally [defeated](/wiki/Defeat_of_the_Sith "Defeat of the Sith") in [1032 BBY](/wiki/1032_BBY "1032 BBY").[[14]](#cite_note-Timelines-14) The armies of the Old Republic[[38]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-38) and [Jedi Knights](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight")[[39]](#cite_note-Bane_Galactic_Files-39) were able to defeat the remaining Sith[[38]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-38) at the [Mid Rim Territories](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories") [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet")[[40]](#cite_note-Visual_Encyclopedia-40) [Ruusan](/wiki/Ruusan "Ruusan")[[41]](#cite_note-Helmet_Collection-41) by taking advantage of the infighting within the Order,[[38]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-38) which proved to be the Sith's undoing.[[41]](#cite_note-Helmet_Collection-41) The Sith abandoned their traditional homeworld of Moraband after it was scarred by many wars,[[42]](#cite_note-datamora-42) and went into hiding.[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5) Very few Sith remained by that point, and they ultimately destroyed themselves. Only one [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") survived; [Darth Bane](/wiki/Darth_Bane "Darth Bane") reinvented the Sith by creating the [Rule of Two](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two"). Henceforth, their ranks were limited to a [Sith Master](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master") and a [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice").[[38]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-38)

 [![The Old Republic was reborn as the modern Galactic Republic after millennia of warfare.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/Galactic_City.png/revision/latest?cb=20130212011759) [![The Old Republic was reborn as the modern Galactic Republic after millennia of warfare.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/Galactic_City.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130212011759)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/Galactic_City.png/revision/latest?cb=20130212011759) 

The Old Republic was reborn as the modern Galactic Republic after millennia of warfare.

 

As the Old Republic fell apart as a result of its continuous wars, the Jedi Order finally believed itself victorious from its conflict with the Sith, who they believed to have been destroyed completely. Finally, with peace restored to the galaxy, the shattered Old Republic reorganized itself into the modern Galactic Republic,[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) which would usher in over one thousand years of stability in an epoch known as the [Great Peace](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era").[[43]](#cite_note-Collapse-43) The story of Old Republic [Regent](/wiki/Regent "Regent") [Hylemane Lightbringer](/wiki/Hylemane_Lightbringer "Hylemane Lightbringer") and his supposed [immortality](/wiki/Immortality "Immortality") would be remembered in history texts along with Old Republic music such as the [Sestina of Imperator Vex](/wiki/Sestina_of_Imperator_Vex "Sestina of Imperator Vex"), which would continue to be sung even in the [months](/wiki/Standard_month "Standard month") following the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor").[[18]](#cite_note-Aftermath-18)

### Rise of democracy[]

:   "*There hasn't been a full-scale war since the formation of the Republic.*"
:   ―Sio Bibble[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9)

 [![The Great Peace of the Republic lasted for almost a thousand years.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/de/Millennial_Celebration_Invitation.png/revision/latest?cb=20180202010839) [![The Great Peace of the Republic lasted for almost a thousand years.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/de/Millennial_Celebration_Invitation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20180202010839)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/de/Millennial_Celebration_Invitation.png/revision/latest?cb=20180202010839) 

The Great Peace of the Republic lasted for almost a thousand years.

 

The Old Republic was restored[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26) in the form of the modern Galactic Republic[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) in 1032 BBY.[[12]](#cite_note-Altdate_and_Restoration_date-12) After the Galactic Republic's reformation,[[29]](#cite_note-Zygerrian_Databank-29) the Zygerrians would continue to hold a grudge against both the Republic and the Jedi Order for the destruction of their slave empire.[[44]](#cite_note-Kidnapped-44)[[45]](#cite_note-Slaves_of_the_Republic-45)[[46]](#cite_note-Escape_from_Kadavo-46)

The modern Republic was a [democratic](/wiki/Democracy "Democracy") union that consisted of multiple [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") spread across the galaxy.[[1]](#cite_note-RepublicDB-1) With the exception of small-scale conflicts that the Jedi dealt with, the Republic Era was an age of peace and stability that lasted for over a [millennium](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium").[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) This version of the Republic existed in a demilitarized state for most of its history;[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9) as such, the government relied on the [Jedi Knights](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight"), who upheld their mandate as the guardians of peace and justice.[[47]](#cite_note-JediDB-47)

The [Four Sages of Dwartii](/wiki/Four_Sages_of_Dwartii "Four Sages of Dwartii") were notable in influencing some of its earliest laws.[[48]](#cite_note-VE-48) As its governing body, the newly reorganized government established the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"), the members of which were elected to represent their systems. Coruscant was the galactic seat of power under the Republic,[[1]](#cite_note-RepublicDB-1) as it had been for thousands of years before the Republic's rebirth.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

The Republic's head of state, the [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor"), was elected by and from the senators, in which the first in a long line of Chancellors[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5) was [Tarsus Valorum](/wiki/Tarsus_Valorum "Tarsus Valorum"),[[8]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Separatists-8) a scion of the [House Valorum](/wiki/House_Valorum "House Valorum").[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5)[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10) Protecting the new democracy was the elite [Senate Guard](/wiki/Senate_Guard "Senate Guard"), who could be seen patrolling the [Senate District](/wiki/Federal_District "Federal District") and came to be seen as symbols of strength and unity, especially considering the fact that the military had been disbanded.[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5)[[49]](#cite_note-SWEsenateguard-49) In time, the Jedi Order, a noble order of protectors who could tap into the power of the Force, came to serve the Republic as guardians of peace and justice.[[47]](#cite_note-JediDB-47) With the lack of a standing army, the Republic came to rely on its peacekeeping [Judicial Forces](/wiki/Judicial_Forces "Judicial Forces"), led by the Judicial Department as the *de facto* [law enforcement](/wiki/Law_enforcement_agency "Law enforcement agency") branch of the government. The Judicial Forces, members of which were simply known as [Judicials](/wiki/Judicial "Judicial"), trained at the [Judicial Academy](/wiki/Judicial_Academy "Judicial Academy") and came to serve in both ground and space forces, often led by Jedi [Commanders](/wiki/Commander "Commander") to maintain peace throughout the galaxy.[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5)

### High Republic Era[]

#### A golden age[]

:   "*We are all the Republic.*"
:   ―Lina Soh[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

 [![The term "High Republic" referred to an era of prosperity and exploration between 500 BBY and 100 BBY.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/High_Republic_symbol.svg/revision/latest?cb=20250517185050) [![The term "High Republic" referred to an era of prosperity and exploration between 500 BBY and 100 BBY.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/High_Republic_symbol.svg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250517185050)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/High_Republic_symbol.svg/revision/latest?cb=20250517185050) 

The term "High Republic" referred to an era of prosperity and exploration between 500 BBY and 100 BBY.

 

With the galaxy at peace,[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6) the [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era"), which lasted from around [500 BBY](/wiki/500_BBY "500 BBY") to around [100 BBY](/wiki/100_BBY "100 BBY"),[[14]](#cite_note-Timelines-14) saw the Galactic Republic reach the pinnacle of its power, with its influence spreading to even the farthest and less settled regions of the galaxy:[[50]](#cite_note-HR_Announcement-50) the Republic worked to expand into the Outer Rim, specifically a region[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6) of the Rim[[51]](#cite_note-Into_the_Dark-51) known as the [Galactic Frontier](/wiki/Galactic_Frontier "Galactic Frontier").[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6) The Jedi Order also became increasingly active in galactic affairs[[52]](#cite_note-Kylo_2-52) and helped the Republic's efforts. An [Office of the Frontier](/wiki/Office_of_the_Frontier "Office of the Frontier") was established.[[53]](#cite_note-Convergence-53) The Republic's expansion kicked off the [Great Hyperspace Rush](/wiki/Great_Hyperspace_Rush "Great Hyperspace Rush") to find and map any yet to be discovered [hyperspace routes](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route"),[[54]](#cite_note-Out_of_the_Shadows-54) with [Republic Pathfinders](/wiki/Republic_Pathfinder "Republic Pathfinder") working directly for the government[[55]](#cite_note-Galactic_Tales_Inheritance-55) as [Outer Rim Exploration Teams](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Exploration_Team "Outer Rim Exploration Team").[[53]](#cite_note-Convergence-53) Private groups got involved in the hunt for new hyperspace routes as well, with the [San Tekka clan](/wiki/San_Tekka_clan "San Tekka clan") and [Graf family](/wiki/Graf_family "Graf family") both taking advantage of the rush. The San Tekka clan's success in locating new routes and ensuing fortune from those discoveries were secretly a result of the Force-sensitive [Mari San Tekka](/wiki/Mari_San_Tekka "Mari San Tekka"), who had the special ability to locate and map out the routes herself.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

Beyond the mission to open up new hyperlanes[[56]](#cite_note-Pathfinders_and_Comms_Teams-56) by discovering[[54]](#cite_note-Out_of_the_Shadows-54) and charting them,[[53]](#cite_note-Convergence-53) Republic Pathfinders were ordered to explore, help those they found, and, in what was a major part of their mission, establish a functioning communications network across the Outer Rim. While creating the network, Pathfinder teams often worked alongside comms teams in order to get in contact with the Republic at large while out in the Rim. However, the Pathfinders needed to establish the network one node at a time. While the Pathfinders knew the long-term effort would one day result in communications being as fast in the Rim as it was in the Core, [Grint Rupar](/wiki/Grint_Rupar "Grint Rupar") of [Outer Rim Expedition Eight-Zero-Seven](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Expedition_Eight-Zero-Seven "Outer Rim Expedition Eight-Zero-Seven") suspected the work would take generations. Nevertheless, Jedi [Porter Engle](/wiki/Porter_Engle "Porter Engle") dubbed it a noble effort that would change lives for the better. Members of the Jedi Order worked side-by-side with Pathfinders, traveling with them and helping in the Republic effort.[[57]](#cite_note-Blade_1-57) One Pathfinder team, while working on charting the hyperlanes near Sullust, discovered the volcanic planet [Tunguray](/wiki/Tunguray "Tunguray") and evacuated its [people](/wiki/Tunguray_(species) "Tunguray (species)") to safety on Coruscant.[[53]](#cite_note-Convergence-53)

 [![Orlen Mollo and Kyong Greylark served as Co-Chancellors of the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/OrlenMolloKyongGreylark-TheChancellors.png/revision/latest?cb=20230206142613) [![Orlen Mollo and Kyong Greylark served as Co-Chancellors of the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/OrlenMolloKyongGreylark-TheChancellors.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230206142613)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/OrlenMolloKyongGreylark-TheChancellors.png/revision/latest?cb=20230206142613) 

Orlen Mollo and Kyong Greylark served as Co-Chancellors of the Galactic Republic.

 

By [382 BBY](/wiki/382_BBY "382 BBY"),[[58]](#cite_note-382_Date-58) leadership of the Republic was split between two chancellors, [Orlen Mollo](/wiki/Orlen_Mollo "Orlen Mollo") and [Kyong Greylark](/wiki/Kyong_Greylark "Kyong Greylark"). Elected and then re-elected together, their joint leadership[[53]](#cite_note-Convergence-53) as Co-Chancellors[[59]](#cite_note-BoJ-59) helped in the Republic's outreach; while the more formal Greylark remained on Coruscant[[60]](#cite_note-The_Chancellors-60) with the Senate, Mollo traveled across the Outer Rim with his [aides](/wiki/Aide "Aide") and crew aboard the [*Alif*-class Longbeam](/wiki/Alif-class_Longbeam "Alif-class Longbeam") *[Paxion](/wiki/Paxion "Paxion")*,[[53]](#cite_note-Convergence-53) adopting a hands on approach to governance[[60]](#cite_note-The_Chancellors-60) to help with expansion and end problems. Having lived through conflict on Mon Cala, Mollo believed he better understood the Outer Rim but trusted in his Co-Chancellor, whom he believed saw the promise in the Outer Rim but not the finer details he could, all the same due to their shared vision: a truly united galaxy.[[53]](#cite_note-Convergence-53)

Ambassador ships like the *Paxion* were also provided with top-of-the-line [protocol droids](/wiki/Protocol_droid "Protocol droid"), with the *Paxion* being given unit [AR-K4](/wiki/AR-K4 "AR-K4").[[53]](#cite_note-Convergence-53) With the Republic aided by the Jedi,[[61]](#cite_note-THR_1-61) the Republic and [Togrutas](/wiki/Togruta "Togruta") engaged in a [conflict](/wiki/Republic-Togruta_conflict "Republic-Togruta conflict") in [Togruta space](/wiki/Togruta_space "Togruta space") that left tensions between both parties.[[62]](#cite_note-Rising_Storm-62) While Greylark believed the [star system](/wiki/Eiram_system "Eiram system") was not ready for their intervention, Mollo traveled to the planets of [Eiram](/wiki/Eiram "Eiram") and [E'ronoh](/wiki/E%27ronoh "E'ronoh"), which were home to a [war](/wiki/Eiram_and_E%27ronoh_War "Eiram and E'ronoh War") he hoped to finally put a stop to. At the same time, a team of Jedi—consisting of Master [Char-Ryl-Roy](/wiki/Char-Ryl-Roy "Char-Ryl-Roy"), Master [Creighton Sun](/wiki/Creighton_Sun "Creighton Sun"), Knight [Gella Nattai](/wiki/Gella_Nattai "Gella Nattai"), and Padawan [Enya Keen](/wiki/Enya_Keen "Enya Keen")—traveled into the system aboard the *[Valiant](/wiki/Valiant "Valiant")* to provide aid to Eiram, only to collide with the *Paxion* amid a [skirmish](/wiki/Skirmish_in_the_Eiram_system "Skirmish in the Eiram system") that had secretly been orchestrated by the [Path of the Open Hand](/wiki/Path_of_the_Open_Hand "Path of the Open Hand") cult under the control of "[the Mother](/wiki/Elecia_Zeveron "Elecia Zeveron")." Despite the rocky opening, Mollo and the Jedi began the peace process between both worlds' royal families aboard the *Paxion*, although progress only truly started to be made when E'ronohi [princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") [Xiri A'lbaran](/wiki/Xiri_A%27lbaran "Xiri A'lbaran") proposed to [Eirami](/wiki/Eirami "Eirami") prince [Phan-tu Zenn](/wiki/Phan-tu_Zenn "Phan-tu Zenn"), thereby setting the stage for a marriage alliance and an unlikely love story.[[53]](#cite_note-Convergence-53)

Meanwhile on Coruscant, Greylark feared Mollo was making a play at a solo-chancellery ahead of the campaign season. In reality, Mollo simply wanted to be the one to bring peace to the system because of his own past surrounded by war. Deep down, Greylark did trust in her fellow Chancellor, but sent her controversial son [Axel Greylark](/wiki/Axel_Greylark "Axel Greylark") to represent her office in the peace proceedings and report back to her. Axel's own dealings with the Path of the Open Hand nearly led to the destruction of the peace process after cult leader [Elecia Zeveron](/wiki/Elecia_Zeveron "Elecia Zeveron") demanded he bring her a [toxin](/wiki/Poison "Poison") developed on Eiram. Amid the successful [Wedding of Phan-tu Zenn and Xiri A'lbaran](/wiki/Wedding_of_Phan-tu_Zenn_and_Xiri_A%27lbaran "Wedding of Phan-tu Zenn and Xiri A'lbaran") officiated by Mollo, Axel's desperation to prevent Zeveron from securing the toxin led to him destroying the [deflector shields](/wiki/Deflector_shield "Deflector shield") around Eiram's capital of [Erasmus](/wiki/Erasmus_Capital_City "Erasmus Capital City"). After Axel's arrest, the royals agreeing to destroy the toxin, and the formal beginning of the peace process, Mollo reminded his fellow Chancellor to trust him, to which Greylark admitted she did and she had simply wanted to trust her son as well.[[53]](#cite_note-Convergence-53)

#### Conflict with the Path[]

:   **Yoda**: "*Speak to the Jedi Council soon, you should. We must explain the happenings on Dalna. All that went wrong.*"
:   **Orlen Mollo**: "*The communications errors. The machinations of the Path. All going back to the failed talks at Jedha. And beyond.*"
:   **Kyong Greylark**: "*But we must also speak to all the things that went right. We could not have defeated the Path without the Jedi.*"
:   **Yoda**: "*And the Jedi could not have defeated the Path without the help of our Republic allies.*"
:   **Orlen Mollo**: "*Yes. It is a lesson well learned, and a strength that the galaxy can draw upon, for centuries to come.*"
:   ―Jedi Grand Master Yoda, Supreme Chancellor Orlen Mollo, and former Chancellor Kyong Greylark reflect on recent events[[63]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-63)

 [![The Republic rushed to Jedha to shut down the battle spurred on by the Path of the Open Hand (violence on Jedha, pictured).](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2e/Battleofjedhastatuefall.png/revision/latest?cb=20230429025800) [![The Republic rushed to Jedha to shut down the battle spurred on by the Path of the Open Hand (violence on Jedha, pictured).](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2e/Battleofjedhastatuefall.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230429025800)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2e/Battleofjedhastatuefall.png/revision/latest?cb=20230429025800) 

The Republic rushed to Jedha to shut down the battle spurred on by the Path of the Open Hand (violence on Jedha, pictured).

 

With it decided the [Eirami](/wiki/Eirami "Eirami") and [E'roni](/wiki/E%27roni "E'roni") representatives would meet on the neutral ground of [Jedha](/wiki/Jedha "Jedha") to form an official treaty, Chancellor Mollo allowed [Morton San Tekka](/wiki/Morton_San_Tekka "Morton San Tekka") to oversee the discussions as neutral arbiter, deciding it would be better than sending a Republic official. However, the interference of the Path and Graf family member [Tilson](/wiki/Tilson_Graf "Tilson Graf") kicked off the [Battle of Jedha](/wiki/Battle_of_Jedha "Battle of Jedha"),[[64]](#cite_note-Battle_of_Jedha-64) shattering any hope of a lasting peace between Eiram and E'ronoh.[[65]](#cite_note-THR_(2022)_6-65) Rushing to Jedha after receiving a transmission from Sun about the collapse of the peace process, a group of Jedi and a [platoon](/wiki/Platoon "Platoon") of [Republic peacekeeping troops](/wiki/Republic_peacekeeping_troop "Republic peacekeeping troop") shut down the battle.[[64]](#cite_note-Battle_of_Jedha-64) The Path was correctly suspected to be behind the carnage, but the Mother publicly blamed everything on rogue acolytes and attempted to clear her order's name by offering a minimum of one million [Zukkels](/wiki/Zukkel "Zukkel") towards rebuilding Jedha City. While the money was accepted, the revelation that a group like the Path had access to such funds caused the Republic to discreetly investigate, quickly discovering that the Mother had ties to wealthy individuals whom she had convinced to fund her cult.[[66]](#cite_note-Vengeance-66)

After the Battle of Jedha, Axel was freed from prison by the Path of the Open Hand and brought to the [Path compound](/wiki/Path_compound "Path compound") on the planet [Dalna](/wiki/Dalna "Dalna"), where he was received by the Mother, who hoped to use Axel to leverage power over the galaxy through his connection with Chancellor Greylark. In the Mother's plan, Mollo, meanwhile, was going to be killed in a supposed accident as he traveled across the Rim.[[63]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-63) Nonetheless, the Mother rallied her followers against the Republic ahead of the looming [Battle of Dalna](/wiki/Night_of_Sorrow "Night of Sorrow"), alleging that the Jedi lorded over the government and galactic media.[[66]](#cite_note-Vengeance-66) After Axel sent a message to his mother requesting her to come to Dalna as part of the Mother's plans, Greylark decided that she needed to support her son as a parent and understood that, should she arrive as Chancellor, the galaxy would be in danger. As such, she relinquished her position as Chancellor, leaving Mollo the sole leader of the Republic, much to his shock.[[63]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-63)

In the name of investigating the Path, Jedi arrived on Dalna[[63]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-63) with the support of the Republic,[[54]](#cite_note-Out_of_the_Shadows-54) which approved of the action and dispatched guards [Priv Ittik](/wiki/Priv_Ittik "Priv Ittik") and [Lu Sweet](/wiki/Lu_Sweet "Lu Sweet") to aid the Jedi. As the incident devolved into a battle, the Jedi would also be aided by anti-Path [Dalnans](/wiki/Dalnan "Dalnan"), but the Jedi were also faced by Force consuming creatures known as the [Nameless](/wiki/Shrikarai "Shrikarai"). In the end, Greylark arrived on Dalna to help her son, and the united militaries of Eiram and E'ronoh arrived in the name of defeating the Path after its efforts to divide them were uncovered. Although the reinforcements shut down the fighting, the high causalities of the battle, which ended with the Path even destroying its own caverns,[[63]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-63) resulted in it being remembered as a massacre[[54]](#cite_note-Out_of_the_Shadows-54) dubbed the Night of Sorrow.[[67]](#cite_note-Mission_to_Disaster-67) From a certain point of view, the massacre had only happened because of the Jedi-Republic partnership,[[54]](#cite_note-Out_of_the_Shadows-54) yet the Jedi and Republic's victory in the battle was seen as proof that partnership between both organizations made the galaxy stronger.[[63]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-63)

 [![The Mother of the Open Hand (center) led her cult (members pictured) against the Republic but failed to overcome the government and Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/41/PathOfTheOpenHandMembersSymbol-CharactersOfSWTHR.png/revision/latest?cb=20221021134015) [![The Mother of the Open Hand (center) led her cult (members pictured) against the Republic but failed to overcome the government and Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/41/PathOfTheOpenHandMembersSymbol-CharactersOfSWTHR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20221021134015)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/41/PathOfTheOpenHandMembersSymbol-CharactersOfSWTHR.png/revision/latest?cb=20221021134015) 

The Mother of the Open Hand (center) led her cult (members pictured) against the Republic but failed to overcome the government and Jedi Order.

 

In the aftermath of the battle, Axel agreed to spend the time he owed in prison and revealed what he knew of the Path's internal workings, although the cult's membership had been shattered and fled across the stars.[[63]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-63) One of its major leaders, [Guide of the Closed Fist](/wiki/Guide_of_the_Closed_Fist "Guide of the Closed Fist") [Marda Ro](/wiki/Marda_Ro "Marda Ro"), escaped the destruction and set about on a new plan for revenge by forming the [Nihil](/wiki/Nihil "Nihil"),[[66]](#cite_note-Vengeance-66) with her plan being carried on by subsequent generations of the [Ro family](/wiki/Ro_family "Ro family").[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6) Jedi Masters Crieghton Sun and Yoda also agreed to cover up all information on the Nameless until more details were discovered. Meanwhile, a new treaty was set to be signed by the now-cooperating peoples of Eiram and E'ronoh. Two weeks after the battle, a ceremony on the union of Eiram and E'ronoh and the opening of a new hyperlane was held on their shared moon by Mollo.[[63]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-63) At some point, the San Tekka clan lost Mari San Tekka to the Ro family, who used her to locate hyperspace [Paths](/wiki/Path "Path") for their own revenge scheme.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

#### The Starlight Beacon program[]

:   "*In the days of the High Republic, the galaxy was not as settled as it is now. Areas like the Outer Rim were dangerous, hard to navigate. So the people of that time built a huge space station at great effort and expense and placed it in the center of the dark zones. It sent out a signal that acted as a sort of beacon, helping travelers find their way. They gave that station an inspiring name, fitting its purpose.*"
:   ―Grek[[68]](#cite_note-SW_2-68)

 [![Supreme Chancellor Lina Soh endeavored to unite the various peoples of the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/TargonSoh.png/revision/latest?cb=20210215021118) [![Supreme Chancellor Lina Soh endeavored to unite the various peoples of the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/TargonSoh.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210215021118)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/TargonSoh.png/revision/latest?cb=20210215021118) 

Supreme Chancellor Lina Soh endeavored to unite the various peoples of the Galactic Republic.

 

In [232 BBY](/wiki/232_BBY "232 BBY")[[69]](#cite_note-HR_Announcement_date-69) the Galactic Republic was under the leadership of Supreme Chancellor [Lina Soh](/wiki/Lina_Soh "Lina Soh")[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6) and Vice Chancellor [Larep Reza](/wiki/Larep_Reza "Larep Reza"), who was a rising star in the Senate and thought to be Soh's apparent successor whenever her term came to its end.[[62]](#cite_note-Rising_Storm-62) To showcase support for all species in its borders, the governmental motto became "We are all the Republic." Under Soh,[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6) the Republic even began to take steps to curb its habit of indulging in bureaucracy when it needed to be instead taking action; even though the issue remained in a lesser form, the Republic took great steps in advancing beyond it.[[70]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-70) At some point the Republic intervened in the [Soikan civil war](/wiki/Soikan_conflict "Soikan conflict") to finally put a stop to the seemingly-endless conflict.[[67]](#cite_note-Mission_to_Disaster-67)

Concurrent to its [outreach program](/wiki/Outreach_program "Outreach program"), the Republic was in the midst of an era where all voices were listened to, creating governance from consensus and a society of culture, inclusion, ambition, and Soh's many [Great Works](/wiki/Great_Works "Great Works"). Among the earliest of these works—which encompassed everything from infrastructure projects to cultural affairs— was the *[Panacea](/wiki/Panacea "Panacea")*, a [*Salvation*-class Republic medical frigate](/wiki/Salvation-class_Republic_medical_frigate "Salvation-class Republic medical frigate") that was deployed to help citizens after various crises; therefore, the [frigate](/wiki/Frigate "Frigate") became a symbol of Republic's dedication to help its citizens. Other planned Great Works included a new treaty between the [Mon Calamari](/wiki/Mon_Calamari "Mon Calamari") and [Quarren](/wiki/Quarren "Quarren"), the [Republic Fair](/wiki/Republic_Fair "Republic Fair"), various communication relays, cementing the understanding of how to cultivate [Bacta](/wiki/Bacta "Bacta"), and various innovations in fields like technology. The greatest of the works was nonetheless [Starlight Beacon](/wiki/Starlight_Beacon "Starlight Beacon"), which was planned to only be the first in a Beacon network that could truly bring the Republic out of the Core.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

 [![The Republic's "Great Works" initiative saw the construction of distant outposts like Starlight Beacon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/RepublicFairPoster.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210507062217) [![The Republic's "Great Works" initiative saw the construction of distant outposts like Starlight Beacon.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/RepublicFairPoster.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20210507062217)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/RepublicFairPoster.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210507062217) 

The Republic's "Great Works" initiative saw the construction of distant outposts like Starlight Beacon.

 

Constructed along with other way stations at considerable expense and effort[[68]](#cite_note-SW_2-68) through many challenges over a long period of time,[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6) Starlight Beacon was designed to expand the Republic's domain to the unexplored "dark zones" of the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories")[[68]](#cite_note-SW_2-68) because Soh pledged to bring that region into the Republic's embrace, hoping the government could actually help the Outer Rim instead of simply flying through it or using it as another place to collect taxes. Beyond using its beacon to guide travelers and its relay to boost local transmissions by a factor of ten, the Beacon was a Republic embassy[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6) within the Galactic Frontier,[[71]](#cite_note-Great_Jedi_Rescue-71) that could serve many other purposes, being a fortress to discourage piracy, a place for cultural showcases, a state-of-the-art medical center, and, in part, a massive [Jedi temple](/wiki/Starlight_Beacon%27s_Jedi_temple "Starlight Beacon's Jedi temple"). The Jedi provided support to the Republic and its projects. The Jedi established outposts on many Outer Rim worlds, ensuring they could explore and protect those who lived without much of a Republic presence.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

Although the Outer Rim was hard to navigate and dangerous to live in,[[68]](#cite_note-SW_2-68) many poor settlers traveled to the region, leaving the overpopulated Core Worlds and Colonies in pursuit of new lives. These dreams for better lives were supported by the Republic, which—although imperfect like all governments—encouraged the hopes of its citizens, whether those hopes be large or small. Additionally, Soh wanted the people of the Republic to know that they all were part of the government, and the Republic began construction of Starlight Beacon to help with its expansion into the Outer Rim. The beacon was the symbol of everything Soh wanted for the Republic, being able to ensure it could truly expand from the Core to be a galactic government. Others in the government preferred the status quo, wanting to save credits in case of future issues, but Soh, having proved to her people the positive effect of coming together, pushed on with her works to bring the Republic into the Rim. Every Senator knew the success of Starlight would bring forth Soh's hopes that future generations could live in prosperity, while its failure would be massive.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

 [![Starships across the galaxy were thrown out of hyperspace in an event known as the Great Hyperspace Disaster.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/61/TheGreatDisaster.png/revision/latest?cb=20240402134034) [![Starships across the galaxy were thrown out of hyperspace in an event known as the Great Hyperspace Disaster.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/61/TheGreatDisaster.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240402134034)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/61/TheGreatDisaster.png/revision/latest?cb=20240402134034) 

Starships across the galaxy were thrown out of hyperspace in an event known as the Great Hyperspace Disaster.

 

Lacking a formal military due to the galaxy's peace, the Republic was protected by a small peacekeeping fleet known as the [Republic Defense Coalition](/wiki/Republic_Defense_Coalition "Republic Defense Coalition"), which was helped by the Jedi Order. Despite the large-scale partnership between them and Republic during the era,[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6) there came to be some Jedi who doubted whether it was truly the will of the Force for them to act so closely with the government. Indeed, Jedi Master [Cohmac Vitus](/wiki/Cohmac_Vitus "Cohmac Vitus") believed it was a Republic and Jedi partnership that had led to the massacre on Dalna[[54]](#cite_note-Out_of_the_Shadows-54) from over a [century](/wiki/Standard_century "Standard century") prior.[[67]](#cite_note-Mission_to_Disaster-67) The partnership between the two parties would only increase when the [Nihil conflict](/wiki/Nihil_conflict "Nihil conflict") began;[[54]](#cite_note-Out_of_the_Shadows-54) the conflict began when starships were abruptly knocked out of hyperspace in a galaxy-wide event known as the [Great Hyperspace Disaster](/wiki/Great_Hyperspace_Disaster "Great Hyperspace Disaster")[[50]](#cite_note-HR_Announcement-50) caused by the [Eye of the Nihil](/wiki/Eye_of_the_Nihil "Eye of the Nihil") [Marchion Ro](/wiki/Marchion_Ro "Marchion Ro"), a member of the Ro family who had destroyed the [transport](/wiki/Transport "Transport") *[Legacy Run](/wiki/Legacy_Run "Legacy Run")* in hyperspace, which made its remains come out of hyperspace in the [Hetzal system](/wiki/Hetzal_system "Hetzal system"), causing a sudden crisis as they rained upon the system. Beyond wanting revenge on the Jedi for secretive, family reasons, Ro had made his move to ensure the [Nihil](/wiki/Nihil "Nihil") raiders could grow beyond what they were currently. With the Republic expanding into the Outer Rim, he knew they would need to change themselves to survive, launching his plot to ensure he could secure leadership over the raiders.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

 [![The Jedi and Republic rushed to the Hetzal system to save it from the Great Disaster.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/FourJediTwoContractorsOneBox.png/revision/latest?cb=20240320061219) [![The Jedi and Republic rushed to the Hetzal system to save it from the Great Disaster.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/FourJediTwoContractorsOneBox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240320061219)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/FourJediTwoContractorsOneBox.png/revision/latest?cb=20240320061219) 

The Jedi and Republic rushed to the Hetzal system to save it from the Great Disaster.

 

The RDC deployed the [*Emissary*-class Republic Cruiser](/wiki/Emissary-class_Republic_Cruiser "Emissary-class Republic Cruiser") *[Third Horizon](/wiki/Third_Horizon "Third Horizon")* to the Hetzal system in response to the [Hetzalian government](/wiki/Hetzalian_government "Hetzalian government")'s [distress signal](/wiki/Distress_signal "Distress signal"). Aboard the ship, Jedi Master [Avar Kriss](/wiki/Avar_Kriss "Avar Kriss") was overseeing the effort, learning through her [Force network](/wiki/Song_of_the_Force "Song of the Force") that some of the fragments raining upon the system contained living beings. She helped lead the effort to rescue the system's refugees and everyone aboard the fragments until she detected a large container of liquid [tibanna](/wiki/Tibanna "Tibanna") threatening the system's [R-class](/wiki/R-class "R-class") star. Kriss and the other Jedi used their combined focus to move the container with the Force, while the RDC continued to focus on evacuating the remaining refugees. The Jedi's effort to move the container was broadcast across the Outer Rim and into the inner Republic worlds by [technician](/wiki/Technician "Technician") [Keven Tarr](/wiki/Keven_Tarr "Keven Tarr"); while he had at first only sent the signal to Chancellor Soh, he did not want his star system to be destroyed without being acknowledged, so the people of the Republic watched the Jedi effort. At first, the Force users failed, but their second attempt moved the container, saving Hetzal and resulting in cheers across the Republic.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

Although the Republic was able to learn the destruction of the *Legacy Run* had been the cause of the disaster, the government remained unaware of why it was destroyed, making Soh fear another disaster could happen in hyperspace. Additionally, the Republic was faced with the [Emergences](/wiki/Emergences "Emergences"); these were when remaining fragments of the *Legacy Run*, which were all continuing to travel throughout hyperspace, exited in an Outer Rim system, resulting in pieces raining down and destroying whatever they hit. The [First Emergence](/wiki/First_Emergence "First Emergence") was at the [Ab Dalis system](/wiki/Ab_Dalis_system "Ab Dalis system"), which was further along the same hyperspace route the *Run* had been traveling on, and these Emergences continued to spread. Thus, Soh feared the Republic could have to cease hyperspace travel, which would separate worlds and effectively end the galactic government. Additionally, the Nihil took advantage of the First Emergence, launching a [raid](/wiki/Attack_on_the_Garello_convoy "Attack on the Garello convoy") on a [convoy](/wiki/Convoy "Convoy") of ships carrying refugees. Nevertheless, because he had caused it, only Ro understood that they were directly responsible for the Great Disaster and its aftershocks.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

#### Conflict with the Nihil[]

:   "*I mean the Republic, building its Starlight Beacon out in my territory. Invading, taking over, with all its rules and laws and particular brand of freedom that isn't free at all. And you Jedi always just behind, absolutely convinced that every action you take is right and good. My family learned that to its cost, long ago.*"
:   ―Eye of the Nihil Marchion Ro[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

Although it was a larger mobilization effort than anything done for sometime, Soh established an RDC [blockade](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade") of various Outer Rim hyperspace routes, intending to protect starships from being destroyed in hyperspace by stopping that travel altogether. The blockade would ultimately be forced to grow as more systems were effected by the Emergences. As predicted by Senator [Izzet Noor](/wiki/Izzet_Noor "Izzet Noor"), who served as the spokesperson in the Senate for the majority of the Outer Rim, the blockade brought strife, as many Rim worlds were not self-sufficient and depended on hyperspace for trade. During a meeting on Coruscant fifteen Emergences into the crisis, Soh had pledged to send [supply ships](/wiki/Supply_ship "Supply ship") into hyperspace if a food crisis grew too dire, although the halting of the trade still had major negative effects for the Rim. During that same meeting, she established that the hyperlanes would remain closed, minus limited transport of essential goods, until they knew more about the crisis before noting she was unwilling to postpone the [dedication of the Starlight Beacon](/wiki/Dedication_of_the_Starlight_Beacon "Dedication of the Starlight Beacon"); it was nearly finished, and she wanted to use the event to showcase a triumph over adversity.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

 [![The Great Disaster precipitated a conflict between the Republic and the Nihil in the Outer Rim Territories.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/df/AuroraThreeAtKur.png/revision/latest?cb=20210212063758) [![The Great Disaster precipitated a conflict between the Republic and the Nihil in the Outer Rim Territories.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/df/AuroraThreeAtKur.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210212063758)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/df/AuroraThreeAtKur.png/revision/latest?cb=20210212063758) 

The Great Disaster precipitated a conflict between the Republic and the Nihil in the Outer Rim Territories.

 

Survivors of the first Emergence and Great Hyperspace Disaster were taken to the yet-to-officially open Starlight for medical treatment. With Starlight due to open in thirty days, Soh gave that as the timeline to solve the Emergence crisis; she did not want to open the way station while the blockade was still ongoing, knowing it would appear as if the Republic could not protect its own people. Due to the blockade, the Nihil's craft became the only ships traveling at lightspeed, making Ro suggest they slow down operations—stating they could attract the attention of the Jedi or RDC—while also sowing the seeds for his takeover, approving the [raid on Elphrona](/wiki/Raid_on_Elphrona "Raid on Elphrona") to ensure a Jedi would be captured. Meanwhile with the Republic, technician Tarr, having tracked the previous Emergences to form a pattern, began to construct a [system](/wiki/Keven_Tarr%27s_navidroid_array "Keven Tarr's navidroid array") of thousands of [navigation droids](/wiki/Nav_droid "Nav droid"), hoping it could be used to predict where future Emergences would be and find the *Legacy Run*'s [black box](/wiki/Black_box "Black box"). Assigned to learn more about the Emergences, Jedi Avar Kriss and [Elzar Mann](/wiki/Elzar_Mann "Elzar Mann") were also directed to meet with the San Tekka Clan on Naboo by Noor, yet [Patriarchs](/wiki/Patriarch "Patriarch") [Vellis](/wiki/Vellis_San_Tekka "Vellis San Tekka") and [Marlowe San Tekka](/wiki/Marlowe_San_Tekka "Marlowe San Tekka") did not disclose any information about Mari, despite realizing her abilities could have caused the crisis and giving the Republic effort other aid.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

The [Republic rescue fleet](/wiki/Republic_rescue_fleet "Republic rescue fleet") was dispatched to the planet [Trymant IV](/wiki/Trymant_IV "Trymant IV") in the wake of an [Emergence](/wiki/Trymant_IV_disaster "Trymant IV disaster") and [Nihil attack](/wiki/Attack_on_Trymant_IV "Attack on Trymant IV").[[72]](#cite_note-HRA_2-72) The Republic effectively assumed the Nihil were destroyed in the [Battle of Kur](/wiki/Battle_of_Kur "Battle of Kur"), but the marauders survived and began to launch their raids on a galaxy-wide scale, instead of remaining in the Outer Rim.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6) The Nihil [attack on Valo](/wiki/Valo_Atrocity "Valo Atrocity") was a major blow to the Republic, although it did give a chance for the Republic and Torgrutas to heal their relations.[[62]](#cite_note-Rising_Storm-62) In the aftermath of the [Battle of Grizal](/wiki/Battle_of_Grizal "Battle of Grizal"), Republic forces rallied under Jedi Master [Emerick Caphtor](/wiki/Emerick_Caphtor "Emerick Caphtor") to [clear out](/wiki/Debacle_on_Vrant_Tarnum "Debacle on Vrant Tarnum") a Nihil base on [Vrant Tarnum](/wiki/Vrant_Tarnum "Vrant Tarnum").[[73]](#cite_note-TOS_1-73) Following the end of the [Drengir crisis](/wiki/Drengir_crisis "Drengir crisis"), the Republic and Jedi were able to focus their efforts on defeating the Nihil through [Operation: Counterstrike](/wiki/Operation:_Counterstrike "Operation: Counterstrike"),[[74]](#cite_note-Tempest_Runner-74) in which the Republic and Jedi moved to wipe out all known Nihil bases. However, the conflict also resulted in the Republic and Jedi growing closer together, with Chancellor Soh and her aides coming to insert themselves into even the Jedi Council's[[54]](#cite_note-Out_of_the_Shadows-54) normally private[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10) meetings.[[54]](#cite_note-Out_of_the_Shadows-54) In secret, the Nihil had also infiltrated the Galactic Senate via Senator [Ghirra Starros](/wiki/Ghirra_Starros "Ghirra Starros") and [Jeni Wataro](/wiki/Jeni_Wataro "Jeni Wataro"), aide to Senator Noor.[[75]](#cite_note-Shadows_Remain-75) In [200 BBY](/wiki/200_BBY "200 BBY"),[[76]](#cite_note-VowDate-76) Jedi [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Sean](/wiki/Sean "Sean") remembered that the Nihil had launched an invasion of the Republic.[[77]](#cite_note-Vow-77)

#### Expansion and stagnation[]

:   "*With eyes toward expansion into the uncharted reaches of the Outer Rim, the traditions of the Core became passé. Opportunity beckoned from beyond the borders of the Mid Rim worlds.*"
:   ―Janyor[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

 [![Commerce guilds generated massive profits by investing in the Republic's expansionist policy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/Invest_Wisely.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180201060748) [![Commerce guilds generated massive profits by investing in the Republic's expansionist policy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/Invest_Wisely.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20180201060748)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/Invest_Wisely.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180201060748) 

Commerce guilds generated massive profits by investing in the Republic's expansionist policy.

 

The light and prosperity of the High Republic Era was fading[[78]](#cite_note-Launchpad_231-78) by [132 BBY](/wiki/132_BBY "132 BBY")[[79]](#cite_note-AcolyteDate-79) and came to its final end around 100 BBY.[[14]](#cite_note-Timelines-14) Still, for centuries, the Galactic Republic had expanded not through force but by quietly exerting a strong magnetic pull towards neighboring systems. The promise of trade with [Core World](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds") markets held many systems in sway, inexorably luring non-member worlds into tighter cooperation with the state body. Despite this, the Republic remained slow to invite new systems into its fold, as the addition of new territories diminished the [political](/wiki/Politics "Politics") power of existing senators. New member states invariably aligned themselves with local galactic power blocs, while most senators who gave the invitations represented systems in the Core. As a result, the Galactic Center represented the beating heart of the Republic that habitually drew wealth and power from the hinterlands, with most senators dismaying at the extension of services and protection to outlying worlds. Consequently, many useful star systems were left waiting—some for centuries—for the body politic to admit their world as a member of the Congress, even though it came at the cost of the body's overall power.[[80]](#cite_note-A_New_Dawn-80)

As time went by the Republic stood firm, becoming increasingly powerful. As a result, the galaxy remained free of any full-scale war for centuries. However, many of the [bureaucrats](/wiki/Bureaucrat "Bureaucrat") and [senators](/wiki/Senator "Senator") that ran the government continued to work for their own profit rather than the common good. Greed, corruption and internal strife slowly began destroying the government from within.[[1]](#cite_note-RepublicDB-1) The Core, revitalized from the destructive conflicts of the past and ravenous for new resources to exploit, embarked on an aggressive colonization policy, exploring, mapping, and settling untouched planets within the Outer Systems, striking deals with or simply overrunning the indigenous populations that stood in their path. Adventurous pioneers found themselves granted permission by Coruscant to settle new territories and establish trading colonies to feed the Core with the goods and raw materials for its continual self-enrichment. Many new systems, finding themselves lacking the funds to mine, process, and ship their products to market, were forced to secure high-interest loans from the [InterGalactic Banking Clan](/wiki/InterGalactic_Banking_Clan "InterGalactic Banking Clan"), whereupon many, unable to repay their debts, found themselves as mere client worlds to the [Muun](/wiki/Muun "Muun") bankers. As time progressed, the laborious task of astrogating by hyperwave beacons—which required numerous reversions to [realspace](/wiki/Realspace "Realspace")—became simplified with the founding of new [hyperlanes](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route"), such as the [Hydian Way](/wiki/Hydian_Way "Hydian Way"). Many systems, eager to benefit from the opportunities offered by charting hyperlanes through their system, sought to influence the Republic Senate to put themselves on the galactic map.[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5)

 [![The peoples of various worlds were influenced by Coruscanti culture and Republic architecture during the reign of the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ae/SenateDistrict-POP.png/revision/latest?cb=20130519183729) [![The peoples of various worlds were influenced by Coruscanti culture and Republic architecture during the reign of the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ae/SenateDistrict-POP.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130519183729)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ae/SenateDistrict-POP.png/revision/latest?cb=20130519183729) 

The peoples of various worlds were influenced by Coruscanti culture and Republic architecture during the reign of the Galactic Republic.

 

Culturally, [Coruscanti](/wiki/Coruscanti "Coruscanti") fashion, art, drama and literature saw receptive audiences across the galaxy. Seeking to impress visitors from the Core, many worlds sought to build lavish mansions that imitated the [architectural style](/wiki/Republic_architecture "Republic architecture") of the Inner Core. Despite this, many Coruscanti looked with disdain on what was in reality nothing more than a gaudy impersonation. To them, these lifeforms on the galaxy's fringes appeared barbaric, with most worlds still lacking weather control or struggling with geological disturbances and food shortages. Additionally, many outlying worlds, lacking the protection of a federal military found themselves continually harassed by numerous [pirates](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") and criminal organizations, further ingraining the long-held view that those from the galaxy's outlying settlements lacked cultural refinement and basic civility.[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5)

A deep-rooted hatred and distrust grew over the centuries between the galaxy's outer fringes and the cosmopolitan Core, with those in the hinterlands gradually coming to believe themselves the victims of social and economic injustices. As a result of the perceived inability of the Judicial Forces in protecting outlying territories, who were often withheld in intervening after many far-flung worlds refused to provide the Core Worlds with profitable deals, the Outer Rim world of [Eriadu](/wiki/Eriadu "Eriadu")—one of the most politically, culturally and economically developed worlds—formed the [Outland Regions Security Force](/wiki/Outland_Regions_Security_Force "Outland Regions Security Force") for the protection of the [Seswenna sector](/wiki/Seswenna_sector "Seswenna sector"). Comprising an amalgam of ships, it was funded primarily by off-world loans and supplied with [laser](/wiki/Laser "Laser") and [ion cannons](/wiki/Ion_cannon "Ion cannon") acquired from arms merchants who had for centuries been ignoring a Republic ban on the sale of weaponry to member worlds. While the Outland Regions Security Force at first lacked success, it soon came to be renowned for its efficiency at dealing with raiders, especially after [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin") was accepted into Outland's anti-piracy task force, in which he was known for outsmarting and outmaneuvering his opponents.[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5)

 [![The Galactic Senate was mired in political corruption during the Republic's final years.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/Galactic_Senate.png/revision/latest?cb=20130118044253) [![The Galactic Senate was mired in political corruption during the Republic's final years.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/Galactic_Senate.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130118044253)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/Galactic_Senate.png/revision/latest?cb=20130118044253) 

The Galactic Senate was mired in political corruption during the Republic's final years.

 

Despite Outland's best efforts, the Outer Rim Territories continued to fall victim to increasing corporate interests from the Core, with the monolithic [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation") expanding its reach in both the Outer Rim and the Galactic Senate by utilizing loopholes in existing free-trade legislation.[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5) By [42 BBY](/wiki/42_BBY "42 BBY"),[[81]](#cite_note-42BBY-81) the Republic was expanding at an unprecedented rate, yet that expansion was largely due to the Federations' interests.[[82]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-82) While a faction known as the [Militarists](/wiki/Militarists "Militarists") emerged in the Senate with hopes of establishing a formal Republic Military at some point,[[8]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Separatists-8) the Senate voted to cut the [Republic Security Force](/wiki/Republic_Security_Force "Republic Security Force")'s trade route defense program, citing cost concerns as the Federation was unwilling to pay whatever taxes would be incurred to pay for the Republic Guard program. Jedi Master Dooku implored the Senate to reconsider, but his objections were shouted down by Senator [Bulgeski](/wiki/Bulgeski "Bulgeski")—whom Dooku would point out had previously called on the Republic Guard for the protection of his own world, [Salliche](/wiki/Salliche "Salliche")—and the Federation's representative. [Chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor "Chancellor") [Skor Kalpana](/wiki/Skor_Kalpana "Skor Kalpana")—who was characterized by Senator [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") as a good, yet also weak, man—also rejected Dooku's suggestion.[[82]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-82)

Shortly before the [Invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo"), a [trade summit](/wiki/Eriadu_Conference "Eriadu Conference") was held on the Outer Rim planet of Eriadu in which Supreme Chancellor [Finis Valorum](/wiki/Finis_Valorum "Finis Valorum") was turned away by Wilhuff Tarkin, who was hoping to reduce the influence of the Chancellor who some already expected to lose the next election in order to support Senator Palpatine, who had earlier helped Tarkin gain entrance into the Judicial Academy and supported his ascension as [Governor of Eriadu](/wiki/Governor_of_Eriadu "Governor of Eriadu").[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5)

### Invasion of Naboo[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main articles: [Invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo") and [Supreme Chancellor Election, 32 BBY](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor_Election,_32_BBY "Supreme Chancellor Election, 32 BBY")

:   "*It is clear to me now that the Republic no longer functions. I pray you will bring sanity and compassion back to the Senate.*"
:   ―Padmé Amidala, to Sheev Palpatine[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10)

 [![The Sith orchestrated the Invasion of Naboo by controlling the leaders of the Trade Federation.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/Sith_Lords_Trade_Federation.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008105922) [![The Sith orchestrated the Invasion of Naboo by controlling the leaders of the Trade Federation.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/Sith_Lords_Trade_Federation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201008105922)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/Sith_Lords_Trade_Federation.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008105922) 

The Sith orchestrated the Invasion of Naboo by controlling the leaders of the Trade Federation.

 

Despite the best efforts of the well-meaning Chancellor Valorum,[[83]](#cite_note-sweVA-83) the Trade Federation [blockaded](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade") Naboo over disputes about [plasma](/wiki/Plasma "Plasma") exports.
