A Judicial force carried Jedi Master [Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn "Qui-Gon Jinn") and Padawan [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") to the *[Saak'ak](/wiki/Saak%27ak "Saak'ak")*, a Trade Federation [*Lucrehulk*-class LH-3210 cargo freighter](/wiki/Lucrehulk-class_LH-3210_cargo_freighter "Lucrehulk-class LH-3210 cargo freighter") to discuss a peaceful resolution to the conflict.[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5) [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious, the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith"), ordered [Viceroy](/wiki/Viceroy "Viceroy") [Nute Gunray](/wiki/Nute_Gunray "Nute Gunray") to invade Naboo ahead of schedule, and to kill the Chancellor's Jedi [ambassadors](/wiki/Ambassador "Ambassador"). [Theed](/wiki/Theed "Theed"), the capital city of Naboo, was swiftly occupied by the [Trade Federation Droid Army](/wiki/Trade_Federation_Droid_Army "Trade Federation Droid Army"). The Jedi, having survived the Federation's efforts to kill them, [escaped](/wiki/Escape_from_the_Saak%27ak "Escape from the Saak'ak") to Naboo where they rescued [Queen](/wiki/Monarch_of_Naboo "Monarch of Naboo") [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") and her entourage.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10)

Amidala undertook a journey to Coruscant to plead her [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld")'s case to the Senate, but the damage to the [Naboo Royal Starship](/wiki/Naboo_Royal_Starship "Naboo Royal Starship")'s [T-14 hyperdrive generator](/wiki/T-14_hyperdrive_generator "T-14 hyperdrive generator") necessitated a detour to the remote world of [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine") for repairs. Acting on Gunray's report, Sidious instructed his [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice"), [Darth Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul"), to locate and reacquire the [queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen") as only she had the authority to sign a treaty making the Federation's occupation of Naboo legal. Although Maul tracked them to Tatooine, he failed to prevent the Jedi from escaping with Amidala on her repaired starship. In addition, Jinn took custody of an emancipated slave child, [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), whom he found to be exceptionally strong with the Force. Believing that he had found the prophesied [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One"), Jinn brought Skywalker to Coruscant to begin his [Jedi training](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training").[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10)

 [![Queen Amidala's Vote of No Confidence was instrumental in Senator Sheev Palpatine's rise to power.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/Amidalabeforesenate.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111008200123) [![Queen Amidala's Vote of No Confidence was instrumental in Senator Sheev Palpatine's rise to power.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/Amidalabeforesenate.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111008200123)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/Amidalabeforesenate.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111008200123) 

Queen Amidala's Vote of No Confidence was instrumental in Senator Sheev Palpatine's rise to power.

 

Senator Palpatine and Chancellor Valorum greeted Amidala upon her arrival to the capital. Though Valorum assured her of the Senate's distress over the situation, Palpatine warned her that neither the Senate nor the Chancellor were likely to intervene unless they made a change in leadership. As Naboo's galactic representative, Palpatine served as Amidala's advisor and confidant. He told her that the Senate was corrupt, and the Chancellor a figurehead to the bureaucrats. When the Trade Federation's delegates forced Valorum to adhere to bureaucratic procedure, Amidala countered by calling for a [Vote of No Confidence](/wiki/Vote_of_No_Confidence "Vote of No Confidence") in him, following Palpatine's advice despite her initial reluctance to denounce a strong supporter of her world.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10)

Believing the Republic no longer adhered to its founding principles, Amidala returned to her planet to liberate the [people of Naboo](/wiki/Naboo_(people) "Naboo (people)") without the Senate's intervention. Before leaving Coruscant, Palpatine informed her of his nomination to succeed Valorum. His competitors were Senator [Bail Antilles](/wiki/Bail_Antilles "Bail Antilles") of Alderaan and Senator [Ainlee Teem](/wiki/Ainlee_Teem "Ainlee Teem") of [Malastare](/wiki/Malastare "Malastare"), but Palpatine assured Amidala that he would win the [election](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor_election,_32_BBY "Supreme Chancellor election, 32 BBY") through widespread sympathy for Naboo's plight. He vowed to dedicate his term to ending corruption, and Amidala implored him to restore compassion to the Senate.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10)

 [![The victors of the Battle of Naboo celebrated their triumph in the liberated city of Theed.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Naboo_celebration.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111008202536) [![The victors of the Battle of Naboo celebrated their triumph in the liberated city of Theed.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Naboo_celebration.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111008202536)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Naboo_celebration.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111008202536) 

The victors of the Battle of Naboo celebrated their triumph in the liberated city of Theed.

 

Unable to count on Republic aid, Amidala turned to Naboo's [Gungan](/wiki/Gungan "Gungan") population. Despite ill feelings between their segregated societies, the occupation of their shared homeworld allowed Amidala to mend their relationship through diplomacy. The [Gungan Grand Army](/wiki/Gungan_Grand_Army "Gungan Grand Army") confronted the Trade Federation's [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid") while the [Naboo Royal Space Fighter Corps](/wiki/Naboo_Royal_Space_Fighter_Corps "Naboo Royal Space Fighter Corps") launched an attack on the *Saak'ak* in orbit. The Gungans were forced to surrender after their defenses collapsed, and several [Naboo Fighter Pilots](/wiki/Naboo_Fighter_Pilot "Naboo Fighter Pilot") were killed in the space battle. However, Amidala's team infiltrated the [Theed Royal Palace](/wiki/Theed_Royal_Palace "Theed Royal Palace") where they captured Gunray, and with the *Saak'ak* destroyed by Skywalker, the droids were deactivated. In the aftermath of the [Battle of Naboo](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo"), Gunray was taken into Republic custody and the newly-elected Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine arrived in Theed where he and the queen congratulated each other on their recent success. The new Chancellor said that they would work together bringing peace and prosperity to the Republic.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10)

### Separatist Crisis[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis")

:   "*I will not let this Republic that has stood for a thousand years be split in two. My negotiations will not fail.*"  
    "*If they do, you must realize that there aren't enough Jedi to protect the Republic. We're keepers of the peace, not soldiers.*"
:   ―Sheev Palpatine and Mace Windu[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9)

 [![The Separatist Crisis reflected widespread disillusionment with the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/63/2000_Senators_propaganda.png/revision/latest?cb=20161022185206) [![The Separatist Crisis reflected widespread disillusionment with the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/63/2000_Senators_propaganda.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20161022185206)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/63/2000_Senators_propaganda.png/revision/latest?cb=20161022185206) 

The Separatist Crisis reflected widespread disillusionment with the Republic.

 

Following the Naboo Crisis, the Trade Federation monopoly on the Outer Rim was broken, all while Supreme Chancellor Finis Valorum's political standing suffered from the crisis along with other scandals. In his wake, Palpatine was appointed to the position of Supreme Chancellor, eventually creating an image of himself as a mild-mannered servant of the common good, despite his true intentions. However, growing tensions between the Core and Outer Rim worlds gradually increased to the point where many believed that a war was imminent.[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5) Foreseeing this conflict years before the Invasion of Naboo, Jedi Master [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas") advocated for the creation of a new Republic army, only to be rejected by the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council"), who believed his ideas too extreme. Undeterred, Sifo-Dyas contacted the [Kaminoans](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan"), known for their [clone](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") hatcheries, and secretly commissioned them to create a clone army, pretending to represent the Galactic Senate. Unbeknownst to Sifo-Dyas, Darth Sidious had earlier contacted [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister "Prime Minister") [Lama Su](/wiki/Lama_Su "Lama Su"), and convinced him to implant a [behavioral modification biochip](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") into the clones during the third stage of their development to turn against the Jedi at a mere command.[[84]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-84)

 [![The former Jedi Master Dooku led the Separatist movement against the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ac/Dooku-GhostsOfTheMachine.png/revision/latest?cb=20221102200953) [![The former Jedi Master Dooku led the Separatist movement against the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ac/Dooku-GhostsOfTheMachine.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20221102200953)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ac/Dooku-GhostsOfTheMachine.png/revision/latest?cb=20221102200953) 

The former Jedi Master Dooku led the Separatist movement against the Republic.

 

The dashing swordsman and political idealist Jedi Master [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku"), taking an eight-[year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") leave of absence from the Jedi Order and now secretly the apprentice of Darth Sidious and dubbed Darth Tyranus,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9) paid the [Pyke Syndicate](/wiki/Pyke_Syndicate "Pyke Syndicate") to eliminate Sifo-Dyas over the planet of [Oba Diah](/wiki/Oba_Diah "Oba Diah"). With Sifo-Dyas originally heading to the planet in order to negotiate a dispute that could have resulted in a full-scale gang war on Coruscant, Sifo-Dyas was suddenly re-assigned to [Felucia](/wiki/Felucia "Felucia") when his shuttle was abruptly shot down over the planet. Bringing his body to Felucia, where it was cremated by tribal inhabitants, Dooku managed to trick the Jedi Council into believing Sifo-Dyas had been killed by the Felucians,[[84]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-84) all while erasing the existence of [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino") from the [Jedi Archives](/wiki/Jedi_Archives "Jedi Archives").[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9)

In the decade after the Invasion of Naboo, the whereabouts of Count Dooku were scarcely known, with many believing he merely wished to form an offshoot of the Jedi Order. In reality, Dooku manipulated galactic events to foment political turmoil on a variety of worlds, including [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk"), [Sullust](/wiki/Sullust "Sullust"), and [Onderon](/wiki/Onderon "Onderon"). Seeking to create a southern Separatist sphere of influence by bringing [Yag'Dhul](/wiki/Yag%27Dhul "Yag'Dhul") and [Sluis Van](/wiki/Sluis_Van "Sluis Van") to his side, Dooku needed to persuade the now prosperous world of Eriadu to join the Separatists. However, Wilhuff Tarkin was pressured to declare his loyalties especially after Dooku commandeered a [HoloNet](/wiki/HoloNet "HoloNet") station in the [Raxus system](/wiki/Raxus_system "Raxus system") and denounced the Galactic Republic, effectively setting the stage for the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis"). Tarkin ultimately sided with the Galactic Republic in his stern belief that an inefficient yet unified galaxy was better than a fractured one.[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5)

 [![The Senate granted the chancellor emergency powers at the behest of Representative Jar Jar Binks.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e2/JarJarDestroysTheRepublic-AotC.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111001150650) [![The Senate granted the chancellor emergency powers at the behest of Representative Jar Jar Binks.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e2/JarJarDestroysTheRepublic-AotC.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111001150650)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e2/JarJarDestroysTheRepublic-AotC.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111001150650) 

The Senate granted the chancellor emergency powers at the behest of Representative Jar Jar Binks.

 

Chancellor Palpatine's negotiations with the Separatists were unsuccessful, leading the Galactic Senate to consider the [Military Creation Act](/wiki/Military_Creation_Act "Military Creation Act"). Senator Amidala led the opposition against the bill, believing it would make war between the Republic and the Separatists inevitable. Following an [assassination attempt](/wiki/Plot_to_assassinate_Senator_Amidala "Plot to assassinate Senator Amidala") on Amidala, the chancellor ordered her to return to Naboo while the Jedi [investigated](/wiki/Mission_to_Kamino_(Separatist_Crisis) "Mission to Kamino (Separatist Crisis)") the plot against her. [Junior Representative](/wiki/Junior_Representative "Junior Representative") [Jar Jar Binks](/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks "Jar Jar Binks") assumed her responsibilities on Coruscant for the duration of Amidala's absence. The Jedi's subsequent discovery of two secret armies, the clones and the [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid"), influenced the Senate's next actions. The [Loyalists](/wiki/Loyalist "Loyalist") agreed that the Republic needed the clone army, yet they felt that the Senate would fail to pass the Military Creation Act before the Separatists' attacked the Republic with their [droid](/wiki/Droid "Droid") forces. When [Vice Chair](/wiki/Vice_Chair "Vice Chair") [Mas Amedda](/wiki/Mas_Amedda "Mas Amedda") suggested that they resolve the crisis by bestowing emergency powers to Chancellor Palpatine, Representative Binks proposed as much to the Senate who passed his bill, allowing Palpatine to officially recognize the clone army as the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic"). A self-proclaimed proponent of democracy and Republic patriot, Palpatine assured the senators that he intended to return the powers that they had given him after the crisis was over.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9)

### The Clone Wars[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars")

:   "*I have to admit that without the clones it would not have been a victory.*"  
    "*Victory? Victory, you say? Master Obi-Wan, not victory. The shroud of the dark side has fallen. Begun, the Clone War has.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Yoda[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9)

 [![The Battle of Geonosis was the first battle in the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/Clone_Army_Charge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160125191812) [![The Battle of Geonosis was the first battle in the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/Clone_Army_Charge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160125191812)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/Clone_Army_Charge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160125191812) 

The Battle of Geonosis was the first battle in the Clone Wars.

 

The Clone Wars began with the [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis"). Supported by the [Republic Navy](/wiki/Republic_Navy "Republic Navy"), the Grand Army of the Republic engaged the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army") in the open field. The Jedi joined the battle as well,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9) acting as *de facto* generals for the clone troopers.[[85]](#cite_note-SW:CL-85) Meanwhile, [Poggle the Lesser](/wiki/Poggle_the_Lesser "Poggle the Lesser")'s schematics for the [Ultimate Weapon](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station") were transferred to Dooku who escaped the battle after [dueling](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel") Skywalker, Kenobi, and [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda"). Simultaneously, the various members of the newly-founded [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") evacuated the planet as Republic clone [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") gradually forced the droid army into full retreat. The battle was hailed as a Republic victory, although Yoda took the opposite position as he knew that war would spread across the galaxy. Count Dooku traveled to an [industrial sector](/wiki/The_Works "The Works") on Coruscant to inform his master that the war had begun as planned, all while the Jedi High Council pondered Dooku's warning that the Dark Lord of the Sith controlled the Senate.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9)

In the aftermath of the Battle of [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis"), the deadly three-year conflict that engulfed the galaxy in chaos officially began.[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26) Though suspicious of Dooku's claim that the Senate was under the Sith's influence,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9) the Jedi continued to serve the Republic. The [military rank](/wiki/Military_rank "Military rank") of [Jedi General](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") was created,[[86]](#cite_note-Mace_Windu_1-86) allowing the Jedi to lead the Grand Army of the Republic in an official capacity.[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26) Early into the war, Sidious learned of a splinter faction in the Trade Federation under the Neimoidian [Oje N'deeb](/wiki/Oje_N%27deeb "Oje N'deeb"), who wanted to usurp Gunray and give the Outer Rim a chance for a new future. While initially outraged and considering crushing the rebellion outright to ensure the Federation and the legacy it would leave behind stayed true to his plans, Sidious quickly realized he could use the upstart to his advantage; if N'deeb's operation was turned to his own ends, the Outer Rim would be strengthened by N'deeb's faction, but that work would only serve to prolong the war. Once the "chance" N'deeb offered the Rim was crushed, furthermore, Sidious understood that its people who feel even more bitter towards the Republic.[[87]](#cite_note-QH-87)

 [![With the galaxy in a state of war, the Jedi became generals in the Grand Army of the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/AnakinAndNautolanJediTeamUp-AORPadme1.png/revision/latest?cb=20210629150426) [![With the galaxy in a state of war, the Jedi became generals in the Grand Army of the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/AnakinAndNautolanJediTeamUp-AORPadme1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210629150426)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/AnakinAndNautolanJediTeamUp-AORPadme1.png/revision/latest?cb=20210629150426) 

With the galaxy in a state of war, the Jedi became generals in the Grand Army of the Republic.

 

The worlds that were caught in the middle of the conflict were forced to choose sides between the Galactic Republic and its clone army or the ever-expanding Confederacy of Independent Systems and its droid army. With the war well under way, numerous diplomatic envoys engaged in several attempts to sway local worlds to join the Galactic Republic, with Jedi Master Yoda seeking to win the support of the [Toydarian](/wiki/Toydarian "Toydarian") [King](/wiki/King "King") [Katuunko](/wiki/Katuunko "Katuunko"), while [Sith assassin](/wiki/Sith_assassin "Sith assassin") [Asajj Ventress](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress "Asajj Ventress") sought to disrupt the meeting, and instead sought to win the support of the king to join the Confederacy.[[88]](#cite_note-Ambush-88) The Republic also sent military aid and support to factions in need, such as [Cham Syndulla](/wiki/Cham_Syndulla "Cham Syndulla")'s [Twi'lek Resistance](/wiki/Twi%27lek_Resistance "Twi'lek Resistance") on [Ryloth](/wiki/Ryloth "Ryloth"),[[89]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-89) or to the [Dugs](/wiki/Dug "Dug") of Malastare, whose lucrative fuel reserves were a great boon to the Republic Navy.[[90]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-90) Numerous worlds such as [Mandalore](/wiki/Mandalore "Mandalore") also attempted to maintain their neutrality, although they often were forced to seek aid from third parties in times of need.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9)[[32]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-32)

Throughout the Clone Wars, numerous attempts were made against Supreme Chancellor Palpatine's life, including an kidnapping attempt on Naboo masterminded by Count Dooku[[91]](#cite_note-Crisis_on_Naboo-91) as well as the hostage taking of members of the Galactic Senate by notorious bounty hunter [Cad Bane](/wiki/Cad_Bane "Cad Bane").[[92]](#cite_note-Hostage_Crisis-92) However, political intrigue fueled not only the conflict, but also advances in weaponry and the development of equipment to enhance existing armed forces. Attempts at biological weapons were launched by Separatist scientist [Nuvo Vindi](/wiki/Nuvo_Vindi "Nuvo Vindi"), who attempted to re-create the ancient [Blue Shadow Virus](/wiki/Blue_Shadow_Virus "Blue Shadow Virus") capable of killing millions across the galaxy,[[93]](#cite_note-Blue_Shadow_Virus-93) while the Republic developed the experimental [electro-proton bomb](/wiki/Electro-proton_bomb "Electro-proton bomb"), which could send out an electric pulse upon detonation capable of deactivating an entire droid army.[[90]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-90)

 [![The Republic transported a Zillo Beast to Coruscant after the Battle of Malastare.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/ZilloBeastBreaksFree-ZBSB.png/revision/latest?cb=20200429022352) [![The Republic transported a Zillo Beast to Coruscant after the Battle of Malastare.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/ZilloBeastBreaksFree-ZBSB.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200429022352)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/ZilloBeastBreaksFree-ZBSB.png/revision/latest?cb=20200429022352) 

The Republic transported a Zillo Beast to Coruscant after the Battle of Malastare.

 

Following the [Battle of Malastare](/wiki/Battle_of_Malastare "Battle of Malastare"), the Republic also attempted to create an impenetrable armor by unlocking the biological secrets of the [Zillo Beast](/wiki/Zillo_Beast "Zillo Beast"), an ancient creature from the [Mid Rim](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories"), only to have the attempt end in failure, sending the beast on a [rampage](/wiki/Zillo_Beast_incident "Zillo Beast incident") across Coruscant. After its death at the hands of a Jedi task force, the beast was secretly cloned by orders from the Supreme Chancellor himself.[[94]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast_Strikes_Back-94) In the meantime, the Republic developed a [stealth ship](/wiki/IPV-2C_Stealth_Corvette "IPV-2C Stealth Corvette") capable of cloaking itself, as well as upgrading its standard [Phase I clone trooper armor](/wiki/Phase_I_clone_trooper_armor "Phase I clone trooper armor") to the more sophisticated [Phase II clone trooper armor](/wiki/Phase_II_clone_trooper_armor "Phase II clone trooper armor") prior to the [Battle of Mon Cala](/wiki/Battle_of_Mon_Cala "Battle of Mon Cala").[[95]](#cite_note-Water_War-95)

 [![Republic clone troopers were the military arm of the Galactic Senate.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ae/Hostage-SWL.png/revision/latest?cb=20201031195756) [![Republic clone troopers were the military arm of the Galactic Senate.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ae/Hostage-SWL.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20201031195756)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ae/Hostage-SWL.png/revision/latest?cb=20201031195756) 

Republic clone troopers were the military arm of the Galactic Senate.

 

The Republic adopted the clone army to defeat the Separatists, but the clone troopers were also at the disposal of the Senate. The [Coruscant Guard](/wiki/Coruscant_Guard "Coruscant Guard") was formed by [clone shock troopers](/wiki/Imperial_shock_trooper "Imperial shock trooper") stationed on the Republic capital;[[96]](#cite_note-CoruscantGuard-96) senatorial delegates were accompanied by clone bodyguards;[[91]](#cite_note-Crisis_on_Naboo-91) and the clones became involved in the Republic's internal disputes by acting as enforcers of the Senate.[[97]](#cite_note-Trespass-97) The Senate Guard still accompanied dignitaries on off-world missions,[[98]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-98) but as the war continued the Coruscant Guard became increasingly responsible for the security of the Supreme Chancellor[[91]](#cite_note-Crisis_on_Naboo-91) and the delegates of the Senate.[[4]](#cite_note-Crisis_at_the_Heart-4)

On one occasion, the Republic deployed a Jedi-led force of clone troopers to [Orto Plutonia](/wiki/Orto_Plutonia "Orto Plutonia") at the behest of one of its members, the [Pantoran Assembly](/wiki/Pantoran_Assembly "Pantoran Assembly"). The government of [Pantora](/wiki/Pantora "Pantora") claimed sovereignty over the planet, which resulted in [open conflict](/wiki/One-Day_War "One-Day War") between the [Pantorans](/wiki/Pantoran "Pantoran") and the native [Talz](/wiki/Talz "Talz"). Although the clones served under the Jedi, they were also beholden to the authority of the Pantoran leader, [Chairman](/wiki/Chairman "Chairman") [Chi Cho](/wiki/Chi_Cho "Chi Cho"), and the Pantoran senator [Riyo Chuchi](/wiki/Riyo_Chuchi "Riyo Chuchi").[[97]](#cite_note-Trespass-97)

### Fall of the Republic[]

:   "*Too late, for what? The Republic to fall? It already has, and you just can't see it! There's no justice, no law, no order except for the one that will replace it!*"
:   ―Maul[[99]](#cite_note-PhantomA-99)

 [![The Jedi Temple was the site of a terrorist attack against the Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/TempleSmoke-Sabotage.png/revision/latest?cb=20131026223030) [![The Jedi Temple was the site of a terrorist attack against the Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/TempleSmoke-Sabotage.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20131026223030)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/TempleSmoke-Sabotage.png/revision/latest?cb=20131026223030) 

The Jedi Temple was the site of a terrorist attack against the Order.

 

The Grand Army of the Republic was led by Jedi Generals throughout the Clone Wars.[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26) While many heroic actions were taken by the Jedi and the troopers under their command, inspiring the public with stories of bravery, war weariness only continued to grow as the years went by.[[80]](#cite_note-A_New_Dawn-80) The Republic citizenry grew to believe that the Jedi had abandoned their role as peacekeepers,[[100]](#cite_note-TJWKTM-100) and staged massive protests outside of the Jedi Temple as a result. Despite their waning influence in the galaxy, the Jedi continued to lead the Republic's forces but sustained many casualties in the process. Their role in the conflict was opposed not only by civilians,[[101]](#cite_note-Sabotage-101) but also the [Republic officer](/wiki/Republic_officer "Republic officer") Wilhuff Tarkin who wanted to revoke the Order's military authority, convinced that the [Jedi Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code") was a hindrance on the Republic war effort.[[102]](#cite_note-Counterattack-102)

Padawan [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee "Barriss Offee") also disagreed with the Order's involvement in the Clone Wars, and staged a [bombing](/wiki/Bombing_of_the_Jedi_Temple_hangar "Bombing of the Jedi Temple hangar") in the Jedi Temple as protest, all while framing [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano") of committing the act before being captured herself.[[103]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-103) The [Separatist Shadowfeed operation](/wiki/Shadowfeed "Shadowfeed"), an attempt by Count Dooku to spread information on Republic defeats, making it appear as though a Separatist victory was inevitable, fueled public anxiety and consequently accelerated the militarization of the Republic over the course of the war.[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5) Palpatine painted the picture of military victory over the CIS being the only way to lead the galaxy to peace, justifying the expansion of the Republic Military in the process.[[104]](#cite_note-Senate_Murders-104)

 [![Chancellor Palpatine's wartime powers made him a dictator in all but name.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/PalpatineRedGuard-TWJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20131029023412) [![Chancellor Palpatine's wartime powers made him a dictator in all but name.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/PalpatineRedGuard-TWJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20131029023412)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/PalpatineRedGuard-TWJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20131029023412) 

Chancellor Palpatine's wartime powers made him a dictator in all but name.

 

The war also served as a means for Palpatine to amass more emergency powers, cementing his position as Supreme Chancellor far longer than it technically allowed, all while continuing to centralize political and military authority within the [Office of the Chancellor](/wiki/Office_of_the_Chancellor "Office of the Chancellor"), which included putting the InterGalactic Banking Clan under the Chancellor's oversight.[[4]](#cite_note-Crisis_at_the_Heart-4) By gaining wartime powers, Chancellor Palpatine was effectively a [dictator](/wiki/Dictatorship "Dictatorship").[[105]](#cite_note-Darth_Sidious_DB-105)

Palpatine used the war as his reasoning for amending the Galactic Constitution multiple times, enshrining greater power in his office through his changes.[[106]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-106) He became the most powerful chancellor since before the [Ruusan Reformations](/wiki/Ruusan_Reformations "Ruusan Reformations"). Under the [Reflex Amendment](/wiki/Reflex_Amendment "Reflex Amendment"), he secured near-total power over the military.[[107]](#cite_note-CotR-107) The [Sector Governance Decree](/wiki/Sector_Governance_Decree "Sector Governance Decree"), passed towards the end of the war, gave [governors](/wiki/Governor "Governor") sent out by Palpatine authority over neighboring star systems, all in the name of the war effort.[[108]](#cite_note-OF84-108)

 [![The Republic invaded  with the goal of bringing a decisive end to the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1d/Battle_of_Utapau.png/revision/latest?cb=20130213233402) [![The Republic invaded  with the goal of bringing a decisive end to the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1d/Battle_of_Utapau.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130213233402)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1d/Battle_of_Utapau.png/revision/latest?cb=20130213233402) 

The Republic invaded [Utapau](/wiki/Utapau "Utapau") with the goal of bringing a decisive end to the Clone Wars.

 

After nearly three years of constant warfare, the war reached its climax during the [Battle of Coruscant](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant"), where both factions engaged in a massive naval and ground battle over the Republic's capital world. The confrontation ultimately saw the Republic dealing a severe blow to the Confederacy with the loss of a portion of its fleet as well as its head of state, Count Dooku, at the hands of Anakin Skywalker. Shortly afterwards, [General](/wiki/General "General") [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous") met his end at the hands of Obi-Wan Kenobi during the [Battle of Utapau](/wiki/Battle_of_Utapau "Battle of Utapau"). Yet even as the Republic pressed on with the Outer Rim Sieges, determined to bring an end to the civil war, the Jedi High Council had grown increasingly wary of Palpatine.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2)

Over the course of the Clone Wars, the Chancellor's wartime authority reached unprecedented levels at the expense of the Senate, some of whom also grew concerned for the future of the Republic. As such, members of the Council and the Senate began to consider their options for the preservation of democracy.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) The [Delegation of 2,000](/wiki/Delegation_of_2,000 "Delegation of 2,000") emerged and sought to [petition](/wiki/Petition_of_2,000 "Petition of 2,000") the Chancellor to relinquish his emergency powers,[[109]](#cite_note-Meena_Tills-109) whereas the Council contemplated the possibility of removing him by force and taking over the Senate in order to secure a peaceful transition of power.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2)

 [![Palpatine was the Sith Lord Darth Sidious, whose machinations brought about the fall of the Jedi and the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/Execute_Order_66.png/revision/latest?cb=20121210185439) [![Palpatine was the Sith Lord Darth Sidious, whose machinations brought about the fall of the Jedi and the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/Execute_Order_66.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121210185439)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/Execute_Order_66.png/revision/latest?cb=20121210185439) 

Palpatine was the Sith Lord Darth Sidious, whose machinations brought about the fall of the Jedi and the Republic.

 

Ultimately, their suspicion of the Chancellor was vindicated when Skywalker uncovered the truth: Sheev Palpatine and Darth Sidious, the Sith mastermind behind the Clone Wars, were one and the same. Realizing they had been deceived by the Chancellor, the Council [attempted to arrest](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") the Sith Lord before his plan could come to fruition, consequently leading to a [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel") in which Sidious struck down [Agen Kolar](/wiki/Agen_Kolar "Agen Kolar"), [Saesee Tiin](/wiki/Saesee_Tiin "Saesee Tiin"), and [Kit Fisto](/wiki/Kit_Fisto "Kit Fisto") before [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu") disarmed him. Given the Chancellor's control over the Senate and the courts, Windu deemed Sidious too dangerous to live. However, Skywalker, despite having performed an execution himself, argued that execution was contrary to the Jedi way, though his personal attachment to Amidala also influenced him at this critical point as he believed that Sidious could save her life.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2)

In a moment of desperation, Skywalker disarmed Windu, which allowed Sidious to kill the Jedi Order's champion with a torrent of [Force lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning"). Having chosen the path of the dark side, the fallen Jedi Knight became Darth Vader and subsequently led the [attack on the Jedi Temple](/wiki/Operation:_Knightfall "Operation: Knightfall") while Sidious issued [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66") to the Grand Army, causing the clone [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") being [brainwashed](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") into betraying and executing their Jedi leaders across the galaxy.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) The execution of Order 66 marked the moment where the destruction of the Republic was inevitable,[[110]](#cite_note-BB_S2-110) although Maul maintained that the Republic had already fallen and the Jedi had simply failed to realize as such.[[111]](#cite_note-TPA-111)

 [![With the Jedi eliminated, Sidious declared himself Emperor of the Galactic Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/Declaration2.png/revision/latest?cb=20130211070942) [![With the Jedi eliminated, Sidious declared himself Emperor of the Galactic Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/Declaration2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130211070942)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/Declaration2.png/revision/latest?cb=20130211070942) 

With the Jedi eliminated, Sidious declared himself Emperor of the Galactic Empire.

 

The Senate held an emergency session at the Chancellor's request. Sidious publicly denounced the Jedi Order; he accused them of plotting to assassinate him in order to take control of the Senate, and by extension, the Republic. Meanwhile, Vader undertook a [mission to Mustafar](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar") where he personally executed the [Separatist Council](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council"), at the behest of Sidious who betrayed and no longer needed them. With the [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") in effect, and the Separatists neutralized, Sidious [proclaimed](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") himself [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor"). The Galactic Republic officially became the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"),[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) and democracy was supplanted by the [fascist](/wiki/Fascism "Fascism") [New Order](/wiki/New_Order "New Order").[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) While many senators cheered and applauded the birth of the Empire, Amidala and Organa quietly lamented the Republic's end. Vader deactivated the droid army soon after killing the Separatist leaders on [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar"). The Clone Wars was over, and its conclusion marked the dawn of the Imperial Era.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2)

### Legacy[]

#### Empire and rebirth[]

:   "*This is Master Obi-Wan Kenobi. I regret to report that both our Jedi Order and the Republic have fallen, with the dark shadow of the Empire rising to take their place. This message is a warning and a reminder for any surviving Jedi: trust in the Force. Do* not *return to the Temple. That time has passed, and our future is uncertain.* Avoid Coruscant*. Avoid detection. Be* secret*… but be* strong*. We will each be challenged: our trust, our faith, our friendships. But we must persevere and, in time, I believe* a new hope *will emerge. May the Force be with you always.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi's warning in the recall signal[[112]](#cite_note-Kanan_2-112)

 [![The Galactic Empire sought to erase all traces of the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/Report_Sedition.png/revision/latest?cb=20170305063027) [![The Galactic Empire sought to erase all traces of the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/Report_Sedition.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20170305063027)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/Report_Sedition.png/revision/latest?cb=20170305063027) 

The Galactic Empire sought to erase all traces of the Galactic Republic.

 

In the decades after the dissolution of the Galactic Republic, numerous individuals still clung to the memory of the now Old Republic and its fabled Jedi warriors, while many individuals who knew the Jedi in person refused to believe the Emperor's account of a "Jedi Rebellion."[[80]](#cite_note-A_New_Dawn-80)[[113]](#cite_note-Heir_to_the_Jedi-113) The Jedi Order that served the Republic would continue its legacy and endure during the Great Jedi Purge.[[18]](#cite_note-Aftermath-18) Having been freed from his control chip by former Jedi [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano") during the [skirmish](/wiki/Skirmish_aboard_the_Tribunal "Skirmish aboard the Tribunal") aboard the [*Venator*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Venator-class_Star_Destroyer "Venator-class Star Destroyer") *[Tribunal](/wiki/Tribunal "Tribunal")*,[[114]](#cite_note-Shattered-114) the former [Clone Captain](/wiki/Clone_Captain "Clone Captain") [Rex](/wiki/Rex "Rex") resolved to fight against the Empire in the name of the Republic, even telling former [Clone Sergeant](/wiki/Clone_Sergeant "Clone Sergeant") [Hunter](/wiki/Hunter "Hunter") that they were living proof that the Republic lived on,[[115]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars-115) and his clone siblings.[[116]](#cite_note-Extraction-116)

Nevertheless, a majority of galactic citizens eventually came to believe and actively support the pro-Imperial view, believing the Republic to have grown weak and corrupt, necessitating Palpatine's rise to power. In order to destroy the memory of the previous government, any visible reminder of the Old Republic was quickly removed, with many organizational changes altering the names of various locales and institutions, while architecture was molded to a [more severe and dark aesthetic](/wiki/Brutalist_(architecture) "Brutalist (architecture)"). With the renowned Galactic Senate being renamed the [Imperial Senate](/wiki/Imperial_Senate "Imperial Senate") and the [Senate Plaza](/wiki/Imperial_Plaza "Imperial Plaza") renamed Imperial Plaza and a giant statue of the Emperor erected in it, one could almost forget the Republic even existed.[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5)

However, the memory of the Republic as a force of freedom and justice could never be fully destroyed as long as those who still believed in it lived, thus spurring numerous resistance movements throughout the Empire's reign such as the [Free Ryloth Movement](/wiki/Free_Ryloth_Movement "Free Ryloth Movement")[[117]](#cite_note-Lords_of_the_Sith-117) and [Berch Teller's rebel cell](/wiki/Berch_Teller%27s_rebel_cell "Berch Teller's rebel cell").[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5) These displays of resistance eventually coalesced into the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") prior to the [Battle of Yavin](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin"), where the Death Star was destroyed.[[19]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-19) Subsequent battles included the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor") which saw the destruction of the [second Death Star](/wiki/DS-2_Death_Star_II_Mobile_Battle_Station "DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station") and the deaths of Sidious and Vader, the latter redeeming himself as Anakin Skywalker.[[118]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-118) In the aftermath of their victory at [Endor](/wiki/Endor "Endor"), the Alliance [declared](/wiki/Declaration_of_a_New_Republic "Declaration of a New Republic") itself the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic") as an ode to the Old Republic.[[18]](#cite_note-Aftermath-18)

 [![After the Emperor's death, the Rebel Alliance was reformed into the New Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/A_New_Dawn-SWP.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170110083833) [![After the Emperor's death, the Rebel Alliance was reformed into the New Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/A_New_Dawn-SWP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20170110083833)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/A_New_Dawn-SWP.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170110083833) 

After the Emperor's death, the Rebel Alliance was reformed into the New Republic.

 

However, the New Republic disavowed some aspects of the Old Republic, particularly the legacy of its final years under the chancellery of Sheev Palpatine.[[119]](#cite_note-Bloodline-119) The word "Supreme" was removed from the title of [Chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor_(New_Republic) "Chancellor (New Republic)"); Coruscant was stripped of its traditional role as the galactic capital, allowing other worlds to host the [restored Galactic Senate](/wiki/New_Republic_Senate "New Republic Senate") on a rotating cycle; and the [Military Disarmament Act](/wiki/Military_Disarmament_Act "Military Disarmament Act") reduced the [New Republic Defense Force](/wiki/New_Republic_Defense_Force "New Republic Defense Force") in the [aftermath](/wiki/Galactic_Concordance "Galactic Concordance") of the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War"). Such efforts succeeded in convincing former Separatist worlds to support the New Republic,[[120]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-120) but also led to political partisanship in the Senate where [Populists](/wiki/Populists "Populists") favored the sovereignty of member worlds while [Centrists](/wiki/Centrists "Centrists") lobbied to increase the central government's power and military spending.[[119]](#cite_note-Bloodline-119) Ultimately, the Centrist worlds seceded from the New Republic and joined the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order"),[[121]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-121) a successor to the Galactic Empire,[[122]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-122) resulting in the [Cold War](/wiki/Cold_War "Cold War") between the two galactic powers.[[121]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-121)

The story of Old Republic [Regent](/wiki/Regent "Regent") [Hylemane Lightbringer](/wiki/Hylemane_Lightbringer "Hylemane Lightbringer") and his supposed [immortality](/wiki/Immortality "Immortality") would be remembered in history texts along with Old Republic music such as the [Sestina of Imperator Vex](/wiki/Sestina_of_Imperator_Vex "Sestina of Imperator Vex"), which would continue to be sung even in the [months](/wiki/Standard_month "Standard month") following the Battle of Endor.[[18]](#cite_note-Aftermath-18)

#### Posterity's judgment[]

:   "*Before the outbreak of war, the twilight of the Republic was an era of distractions, with citizens from all walks of life following escapist pursuits. Historians rebuke the people of this last age for being taken in by such circuses when their attentions should have been focused on the malfeasances and corruption in the Senate and other governing institutions.*"
:   ―Janyor[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

 [![Historians rebuked the generation that witnessed the Republic's downfall, holding the people of this last era of peace responsible for the death of liberty.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d4/Coruscant_wealthy.png/revision/latest?cb=20140729221423) [![Historians rebuked the generation that witnessed the Republic's downfall, holding the people of this last era of peace responsible for the death of liberty.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d4/Coruscant_wealthy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140729221423)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d4/Coruscant_wealthy.png/revision/latest?cb=20140729221423) 

Historians rebuked the generation that witnessed the Republic's downfall, holding the people of this last era of peace responsible for the death of liberty.

 

Hailed as one of the greatest political achievements in the galaxy's history,[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26) the Galactic Republic was described by the historian [Janyor](/wiki/Janyor "Janyor") as "the Republic of legend, greater than distance or time." Although other versions existed in the ancient past, collectively known as the "Old Republic," posterity credited the modern Republic for delivering the galaxy from an age of darkness and, with the help of the Jedi Order, forging an era of peace that lasted for a thousand years until the advent of the Clone Wars. Historians romanticized the Age of the Republic, calling it the "last era of peace"—notwithstanding isolated conflicts, which were notably few and swiftly resolved by Jedi mediators—before the rise of vast warships and planet-killing superweapons.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

The Republic in its final years, however, was remembered with less fondness. Historians regarded the people of that time as a generation of apathy and indolence, in which galactic senators cared more about power and luxury than representing their constituents or addressing the perceived inefficiencies of the government. The civilian population was also seen as a contributing factor to the Republic's demise, with Core Worlders being more invested in podracing events in the distant Outer Rim Territories than the politics that caused dissatisfaction to fester and grow into the Separatist Crisis. Ultimately, historians rebuked this generation and held it responsible for the collapse of the "comfortable civilization" that defined the modern Galactic Republic.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

## Organization[]

### Politics[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main articles: [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor"), [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"), [Judicial Department](/wiki/Judicial_Department "Judicial Department") and [Apprentice Legislature](/wiki/Apprentice_Legislature "Apprentice Legislature")

:   "*It's been my experience that senators are only focused on pleasing those who fund their campaigns—and they are more than willing to forget the niceties of democracy to get those funds.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9)

 [![The Supreme Chancellor was the elected leader of the Galactic Senate.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/Parade.png/revision/latest?cb=20180211191423) [![The Supreme Chancellor was the elected leader of the Galactic Senate.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/Parade.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180211191423)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/Parade.png/revision/latest?cb=20180211191423) 

The Supreme Chancellor was the elected leader of the Galactic Senate.

 

The institutions of the Galactic Republic consisted of the Office of the Chancellor, the Galactic Senate, and the Judicial Department. Executive power was vested in the Supreme Chancellor, although this office was largely powerless and hampered by bureaucratic procedure, particularly during the chancellery of Finis Valorum. Nevertheless, the Chancellor had the authority to issue executive orders summoning the Senate to an emergency session[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10) or sending senators away from Coruscant for security reasons.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9)

The chancellery of Sheev Palpatine shifted the balance of power in favor of the Chancellor's office, a consequence of the wartime powers that the Senate gave its leader on the eve of the Clone Wars.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9) As the conflict spread across the galaxy, Palpatine's chancellery gradually morphed into a dictatorship[[105]](#cite_note-Darth_Sidious_DB-105) with control over both the Senate and the [Republic courts](/wiki/Republic_courts "Republic courts"). Near the war's end, Palpatine appointed Anakin Skywalker as his own personal representative on the Jedi High Council, which the Jedi considered an overreaching exercise of the Chancellor's authority. By then, Palpatine had managed to remain in power by exceeding the term limits of his office, an action that the Senate supported.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2)

 [![The Galactic Senate was the governing body of the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/Reduced_Military_Spending_Bill.png/revision/latest?cb=20120909060835) [![The Galactic Senate was the governing body of the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/Reduced_Military_Spending_Bill.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120909060835)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/Reduced_Military_Spending_Bill.png/revision/latest?cb=20120909060835) 

The Galactic Senate was the governing body of the Republic.

 

Prior to Palpatine's rise to power, the Galactic Senate was the legislative body of the Republic. Many member worlds across the galaxy were represented in the Senate which was headquartered on Coruscant, capital of the Republic.[[123]](#cite_note-Senate_DB-123) At it height, the Senate's power eclipsed that of the Supreme Chancellor[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10) but it had also become stagnant under unbridled corruption and layers of bureaucracy.[[123]](#cite_note-Senate_DB-123) As more politicians grew enamored with the comforts of their office, prioritizing power and wealth over their constituents' needs, average citizens questioned if the Republic and its high taxes were worth the membership.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) The Jedi had also grown distrustful towards senators and regarded their motives with skepticism,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9) notwithstanding the Order's allegiance to the Senate as a whole.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2)

 [![Conflicting ideologies led to factionalism, intrigue, and murder in the Senate.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Onacondafarrdead.png/revision/latest?cb=20120909030948) [![Conflicting ideologies led to factionalism, intrigue, and murder in the Senate.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Onacondafarrdead.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120909030948)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Onacondafarrdead.png/revision/latest?cb=20120909030948) 

Conflicting ideologies led to factionalism, intrigue, and murder in the Senate.

 

With the Senate hamstrung by political infighting and a strict adherence to protocol, it failed to bring swift resolutions to either the Invasion of Naboo[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10) or the Separatist Crisis.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9) In lieu of a diplomatic solution, the Senate rallied under Chancellor Palpatine's leadership. However, the decision to grant him emergency powers eroded their authority, allowing Palpatine to amass even more power at the expense of the Senate. At the time of the Clone Wars, the Senate was divided between supporters of the war effort and pacifists who sought a peaceful end to the fighting.[[123]](#cite_note-Senate_DB-123)

The Judicial Department was an umbrella department over the Republic courts, including the [Supreme Court](/wiki/Supreme_Court "Supreme Court"), the highest court of law in the Republic.[[8]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Separatists-8) Its authority also extended over the Judicial Forces[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5) and the [Republic Office of Criminal Investigations](/wiki/Republic_Office_of_Criminal_Investigations "Republic Office of Criminal Investigations").[[8]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Separatists-8) Like its legislative counterpart, however, the courts were mired by a stagnant bureaucracy and was known to be even more indecisive than the Senate.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10) Despite the arrest of Nute Gunray, multiple trials in the Supreme Court failed to remove him as leader of the Trade Federation to the dismay of the Naboo government.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9)

 [![Clone troopers were used as tools of political propaganda during the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/Unite.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180131041145) [![Clone troopers were used as tools of political propaganda during the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/Unite.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20180131041145)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/Unite.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180131041145) 

Clone troopers were used as tools of political propaganda during the Clone Wars.

 

[Propaganda](/wiki/Propaganda "Propaganda") in the Galactic Republic had long served to sway public opinion in favor of Republic policies, from expanding into the Outer Rim Territories, to waging a pan-galactic war against the Separatists. One such propaganda tool was the [Commission for the Protection of the Republic](/wiki/Commission_for_the_Protection_of_the_Republic "Commission for the Protection of the Republic") (COMPOR). Formed in the early days of the Clone Wars, COMPOR existed as a pro-Republic populist movement. As such, the organization's mission was twofold: to promote patriotism in the Republic, and to brand the Separatists as traitors. This goal was achieved through the [artwork](/wiki/Painting "Painting") of [Donclode Onstruss](/wiki/Donclode_Onstruss "Donclode Onstruss"), [Hamma Elad](/wiki/Hamma_Elad "Hamma Elad"), and other [artists](/wiki/Artist "Artist") associated with COMPOR.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

Throughout the conflict, COMPOR propagandists sought to sustain the war effort by keeping public opinion on the side of the Republic's military forces and their commander-in-chief, respectively the clone army and Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine. Following an [early attempt](/wiki/Jedi_Unite_for_Peace "Jedi Unite for Peace") to utilize the Jedi Order as a propaganda tool, COMPOR focused increasingly on the Grand Army of the Republic, portraying clone troopers as a symbol of [unity](/wiki/Unite "Unite") that the citizenry was encouraged to [support](/wiki/Support_the_Boys_in_White "Support the Boys in White"). In regard to the Separatists, COMPOR depicted their leaders as icons of "[evil](/wiki/Evil_Has_Its_Eyes_On_You "Evil Has Its Eyes On You")," specifically General Grievous and Count Dooku. Using loyalty to the Republic and fear of the Separatists, COMPOR lobbied the Galactic Senate to give more emergency powers to Chancellor Palpatine whom they supported as a [wartime leader](/wiki/Do_Not_Bind_His_Hands "Do Not Bind His Hands").[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

The Galactic Republic also founded[[124]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-124) the [Apprentice Legislature](/wiki/Apprentice_Legislature "Apprentice Legislature"),[[125]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-125) also known as the Junior Senate,[[126]](#cite_note-Kenobi_I-126) for politically minded youth[[124]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-124) who wished for a future career in politics. The Apprentice Legislature were given several real issues to deal with but were minor and weren't security issues.[[125]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-125) Padmé Amidala, the last Republic senator of Naboo, was an [Apprentice Legislator](/wiki/Apprentice_Legislator "Apprentice Legislator") at eight years old.[[124]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-124) The Apprentice Legislature would also exist under the Republic's successor, the Galactic Empire, though by [3 BBY](/wiki/3_BBY "3 BBY")[[127]](#cite_note-PoA_date-127) only forty worlds still sent representatives to the Legislature.[[125]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-125)

### Political divisions[]

:   "*The chair recognizes the senator from the sovereign system of Naboo.*"
:   ―Finis Valorum[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10)

 [![The countless worlds of the Galactic Republic were allowed to retain their individual sovereignty, to which they shared with the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/Palpatine_on_balcony.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141103101206) [![The countless worlds of the Galactic Republic were allowed to retain their individual sovereignty, to which they shared with the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/Palpatine_on_balcony.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141103101206)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/Palpatine_on_balcony.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141103101206) 

The countless worlds of the Galactic Republic were allowed to retain their individual sovereignty, to which they shared with the Galactic Republic.

 

All political entities in the Galactic Republic were fully sovereign, and thereby shared in the privileges and obligations that came with being part of the Republic. Corporations and guilds were also allowed to join the Republic, who all sent democratically elected representatives on behalf of their governments or trade groups from across the galaxy, to the Galactic Senate.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10)

A [series of treaties](/wiki/Republic_Defense_Coalition_treaties "Republic Defense Coalition treaties") between various entities which governed the existence of the Republic Defense Coalition during the High Republic Era. They included defense provisions which required Republic members, such as Chandrila and Alderaan to loan military assets such as starships and personnel for as long as they were needed, after which they were returned to their homeworlds.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

As one of the consequences of the [Military Creation Act](/wiki/Military_Creation_Act "Military Creation Act"), the [Corellia system](/wiki/Corellian_system "Corellian system"), one of the founding systems of the Galactic Republic, was able to close its borders, but without withdrawing from the Republic during the Separatist Crisis.[[128]](#cite_note-Emperor_Palpatine-128)

### Foreign policy[]

:   "*If we are successful, you'll have Maul and I'll have Mandalore.*"  
    "*If Republic forces aid you in your assault, it will break treaties that are a hundred years old. We will effectively be drawn into yet another war.*"
:   ―Bo-Katan Kryze and Obi-Wan Kenobi[[129]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-129)

 [![The Republic intervened in the internal conflict of an independent world, believing Carnelion IV possessed valuable resources.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/RepublicDiplomaticFleet-ObiWanAnakin5.png/revision/latest?cb=20200901040103) [![The Republic intervened in the internal conflict of an independent world, believing Carnelion IV possessed valuable resources.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/RepublicDiplomaticFleet-ObiWanAnakin5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200901040103)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/RepublicDiplomaticFleet-ObiWanAnakin5.png/revision/latest?cb=20200901040103) 

The Republic intervened in the internal conflict of an independent world, believing Carnelion IV possessed valuable resources.

 

The Senate did not intervene in the [Open-Closed war](/wiki/Open-Closed_War "Open-Closed War") on [Carnelion IV](/wiki/Carnelion_IV "Carnelion IV") because the planet was not part of the Galactic Republic. Carnelion IV did not join the Republic because the Senate had little economic interests in the planet.[[130]](#cite_note-O&A1-130) The Republic's diplomatic fleet subsequently forced a ceasefire to the Open-Closed war after Kenobi claimed that the planet had high concentrations of [tibanna](/wiki/Tibanna "Tibanna") gas in its atmosphere in order to bring an end to the long-running conflict.[[131]](#cite_note-O&A5-131)

During the Clone Wars, the Republic tolerated the political stance of neutral governments, among which were the [New Mandalorians](/wiki/New_Mandalorians "New Mandalorians").[[32]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-32) Their leader, [Duchess](/wiki/Duchess "Duchess") [Satine Kryze](/wiki/Satine_Kryze "Satine Kryze"), was a staunch pacifist who sought to keep her homeworld and it allies out of the conflict through her capacity as head of the [Council of Neutral Systems](/wiki/Council_of_Neutral_Systems "Council of Neutral Systems").[[132]](#cite_note-Voyage_of_Temptation-132) The Republic and Mandalore coexisted through treaties over a century old by the time of the Clone Wars,[[129]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-129) though by then the Senate sanctioned a [plan to invade](/wiki/Mandalore_Defense_Resolution "Mandalore Defense Resolution") the planet Mandalore, having grown to believe that Kryze's pacifist government could not protect the Mandalorian people from the [Death Watch](/wiki/Death_Watch "Death Watch") movement. However, the invasion was called off due to evidence that the Senate's pretext for war—the testimony of [Deputy Minister](/wiki/Deputy_Minister "Deputy Minister") [Jerec](/wiki/Jerec "Jerec")—had been falsified.[[133]](#cite_note-DoM-133)

 [![The neutral world of Mandalore hosted a failed peace conference between the Republic and the Separatists.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1d/Peace_conference.png/revision/latest?cb=20121211042616) [![The neutral world of Mandalore hosted a failed peace conference between the Republic and the Separatists.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1d/Peace_conference.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121211042616)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1d/Peace_conference.png/revision/latest?cb=20121211042616) 

The neutral world of Mandalore hosted a failed peace conference between the Republic and the Separatists.

 

Mandalore was the site of attempted peace talks between the Galactic Republic and the Confederacy of Independent Systems, with Duchess Satine overseeing the [conference](/wiki/Confederate%E2%80%93Republic_peace_conference "Confederate–Republic peace conference"). Both governments dispatched their delegates to the neutral world in addition to Republic [Senate Commandos](/wiki/Senate_Commando "Senate Commando") and Separatist [BX-series droid commandos](/wiki/BX-series_droid_commando "BX-series droid commando"). Negotiations broke down, however, allowing the war to continue without interruption.[[98]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-98)

During the war, although Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine claimed that the Republic was willing to assist a neutral star system during their times of crisis,[[134]](#cite_note-The_Disappeared,_Part_I-134) the Senate[[135]](#cite_note-Kenobi's_Shadow-135) and the Republic as a whole[[129]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-129) almost always declined aid,[[135]](#cite_note-Kenobi's_Shadow-135) particularly military aid, to neutral governments as a matter of policy.[[129]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-129) If a government broke its neutrality by siding with the Separatist Alliance, it risked becoming an enemy of the Republic. When the InterGalactic Banking Clan began favoring the Separatists at the Republic's expense, the Republic retaliated by deploying an invasion force to [occupy](/wiki/Invasion_of_Scipio "Invasion of Scipio") the planet [Scipio](/wiki/Scipio "Scipio").[[4]](#cite_note-Crisis_at_the_Heart-4)

 [![Mitth'raw'nuruodo did not see the Galactic Republic as a suitable ally for the Chiss Ascendancy, despite working with Anakin Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Thrawn_Alliances_Anakin_art.png/revision/latest?cb=20200223163431) [![Mitth'raw'nuruodo did not see the Galactic Republic as a suitable ally for the Chiss Ascendancy, despite working with Anakin Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Thrawn_Alliances_Anakin_art.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200223163431)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Thrawn_Alliances_Anakin_art.png/revision/latest?cb=20200223163431) 

Mitth'raw'nuruodo did not see the Galactic Republic as a suitable ally for the Chiss Ascendancy, despite working with Anakin Skywalker.

 

Despite Mandalore's neutrality, Ahsoka Tano and [Bo-Katan Kryze](/wiki/Bo-Katan_Kryze "Bo-Katan Kryze") requested the Grand Army's support to depose the [Shadow Collective](/wiki/Shadow_Collective "Shadow Collective") that [supplanted](/wiki/Takeover_of_Mandalore "Takeover of Mandalore") Satine Kryze's regime. Although the Jedi were concerned about getting drawn into the [Mandalorian civil war](/wiki/Mandalorian_Civil_War_(19_BBY) "Mandalorian Civil War (19 BBY)") while in the midst of the ongoing Clone Wars, especially when the world in question was still officially neutral, they permitted a [division](/wiki/332nd_Division "332nd Division") of the [501st Legion](/wiki/501st_Legion "501st Legion") to support the [Mandalore resistance](/wiki/Mandalore_resistance "Mandalore resistance") in the [Siege of Mandalore](/wiki/Siege_of_Mandalore "Siege of Mandalore").[[129]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-129)

During the Clone Wars, the Republic made indirect contact with the [Chiss Ascendancy](/wiki/Chiss_Ascendancy "Chiss Ascendancy") through Jedi General Anakin Skywalker's encounter with [Senior Captain](/wiki/Senior_Captain "Senior Captain") [Mitth'raw'nuruodo](/wiki/Mitth%27raw%27nuruodo "Mitth'raw'nuruodo") "Thrawn," an officer of the [Chiss Expansionary Defense Fleet](/wiki/Chiss_Expansionary_Defense_Fleet "Chiss Expansionary Defense Fleet"). Thrawn had been tasked with exploring the Outer Rim by the time the Ascendancy, having discovered a mysterious threat in the Unknown Regions, sought to assess the Galactic Republic as a potential ally. Thrawn gathered intelligence on the Clone Wars through his interaction with Skywalker, who, in turn, recruited the [Chiss](/wiki/Chiss "Chiss") officer's help with rescuing Senator Padmé Amidala. Skywalker was impressed by Thrawn during their time working together, which he later reported to Chancellor Palpatine. Thrawn was unimpressed by the Republic, however, believing democracy to be an inefficient form of government.[[136]](#cite_note-Thrawn-136)

### Defense[]

#### Republic Defense Coalition[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Republic Defense Coalition](/wiki/Republic_Defense_Coalition "Republic Defense Coalition")

 [![The Republic Defense Coalition was an interplanetary alliance between the Republic's member worlds.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/HetzalSystem.png/revision/latest?cb=20240320061935) [![The Republic Defense Coalition was an interplanetary alliance between the Republic's member worlds.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/HetzalSystem.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20240320061935)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/HetzalSystem.png/revision/latest?cb=20240320061935) 

The Republic Defense Coalition was an interplanetary alliance between the Republic's member worlds.

 

The Republic Defense Coalition, also known as the RDC, was organized as a small peacekeeping fleet that defended the Galactic Republic's interests during the High Republic Era. The RDC was bound together as an organization through defense treaties signed by the Republic's member worlds, including Alderaan and Chandrila. The treaties that created the RDC gave it the ability to allocate starships and personnel from the signatory worlds in times of emergency. These resources would remain under the RDC's control until the threat was neutralized, after which they would be returned to their homeworlds.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6) The Republic also maintained formations of Republic peacekeeping troops, who were deployed to quell conflicts in Republic territory.[[64]](#cite_note-Battle_of_Jedha-64)

The fleet consisted of several starship types, such as *Emissary*-class cruisers, [*Pacifier*-class sector patrol cruisers](/wiki/Pacifier-class_sector_patrol_cruiser "Pacifier-class sector patrol cruiser"), [Longbeam cruisers](/wiki/Longbeam-class_corvette "Longbeam-class corvette"), and [Z-28 Skywing](/wiki/Z-28_Skywing "Z-28 Skywing") starfighters. Despite the existence of the RDC, the Republic was at the height of an era of peace that had lasted for centuries, with neither the Hutts nor the Mandalorians posing a threat. As a result, the *Emissary*-class resembled a work of art, its crenellations and spires designed to be symbolic of the Republic in a state of tranquility. The RDC operated alongside the Jedi Order as well, allowing the peacekeepers to store their personalized starfighters, the [Jedi Vectors](/wiki/Jedi_Vector "Jedi Vector"), in the hangars of its *Emissary*-class cruisers.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6) The Republic rescue fleet was also maintained at the time of the High Republic.[[72]](#cite_note-HRA_2-72)

#### Judicial Forces[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Judicial Forces](/wiki/Judicial_Forces "Judicial Forces")

:   "*The Judicials are at the end of their tenure, in any case, as the Jedi seem to have become the Senate's arbiters of choice.*"
:   ―Sheev Palpatine, to Wilhuff Tarkin[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5)

 [![Judicials were non-Jedi peace officers of the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/53/Williams_and_Madakor.png/revision/latest?cb=20190911223848) [![Judicials were non-Jedi peace officers of the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/53/Williams_and_Madakor.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190911223848)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/53/Williams_and_Madakor.png/revision/latest?cb=20190911223848) 

Judicials were non-Jedi peace officers of the Republic.

 

The Judicial Forces were the armed peacekeeping forces of the Galactic Republic [Judicial Department](/wiki/Judicial_Department "Judicial Department").[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5) While the Jedi helped to maintain order and peace under the authority of the Galactic Senate, they were not considered a standing military.[[130]](#cite_note-O&A1-130) As officers of the government, Judicials had access to [*Consular*-class space cruisers](/wiki/Consular-class_light_cruiser "Consular-class light cruiser").[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10) The distinctive design and color of Republic cruisers identified them as diplomatic vessels,[[137]](#cite_note-Republic_Cruiser_SWE-137) often used by delegates of the Galactic Senate, agents of the Supreme Chancellor, or members of the Jedi Order.[[138]](#cite_note-Republic_Cruiser_DB-138)

In the last decades of the Republic, the Jedi effectively supplanted the Judicial Forces as arbiters of the Senate.[[5]](#cite_note-Tarkin-5) Judicials therefore acted in a supporting capacity, escorting Jedi ambassadors on their offworld missions.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10)

#### Republic Military[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main articles: [Republic Military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military"), [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic") and [Galactic Republic Navy](/wiki/Galactic_Republic_Navy "Galactic Republic Navy")

:   "*As my first act with this new authority, I will create a Grand Army of the Republic to counter the increasing threats of the Separatists.*"
:   ―Sheev Palpatine[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9)

 [![The Grand Army of the Republic was composed of clone troopers.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Grand_army_formation.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090918154725) [![The Grand Army of the Republic was composed of clone troopers.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Grand_army_formation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090918154725)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Grand_army_formation.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090918154725) 

The Grand Army of the Republic was composed of clone troopers.

 

Towards the end of the Separatist Crisis, the Galactic Senate passed the Military Creation Act, which led to the creation of the Grand Army of the Republic and the Republic Navy.[[8]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Separatists-8) Outfitted with [armor](/wiki/Clone_trooper_armor "Clone trooper armor") weapons and gear,[[139]](#cite_note-ArmorDB-139) clone troopers were the backbone of the Republic Military. Bred for loyalty and combat, clones symbolized the future of galactic warfare at the time of the Clone Wars, the conflict that derived its name from their ranks. The training that they experienced molded the clone troopers into a highly efficient army,[[140]](#cite_note-ClonesDB-140) and because they retained the ability to think creatively despite their stunted independence,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9) they were considered far superior to their droid counterparts. In their first battle against the Separatist Droid Army, the Grand Army displayed a level of military strength unseen in the history of the galaxy.[[140]](#cite_note-ClonesDB-140)
