 [![Clone troopers served under the command of Jedi Generals.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/Jedi_Generals_Geonosis.png/revision/latest?cb=20180623160838) [![Clone troopers served under the command of Jedi Generals.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/Jedi_Generals_Geonosis.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180623160838)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/Jedi_Generals_Geonosis.png/revision/latest?cb=20180623160838) 

Clone troopers served under the command of Jedi Generals.

 

Clones were, by and large, proud to serve as soldiers of the Galactic Republic. Although a minority committed treasonous acts such as desertion or espionage for the Separatists, most were steadfast in their allegiance and many troopers sacrificed themselves for the Republic. They were loyal to the Supreme Chancellor, but also the Jedi who served as generals in the Grand Army of the Republic.[[140]](#cite_note-ClonesDB-140) A strong sense of trust developed between Jedi generals and clone commanders over the long campaigns of the Clone Wars.[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26)

There were several types of clone soldiers that stood as a breed apart from their rank-and-file brethren. The [Advanced Recon Commandos](/wiki/Advanced_Recon_Commando "Advanced Recon Commando"), for example, were noted for their elite status and capacity for independent thinking. Another specialized class was the [clone commando](/wiki/Clone_commando "Clone commando")—elite operatives trained for missions too complex for other soldiers.[[139]](#cite_note-ArmorDB-139)

 [![The Republic Navy utilized Venator-class Star Destroyers as capital ships.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/Anaxes_Republic_Navy.png/revision/latest?cb=20200515144531) [![The Republic Navy utilized Venator-class Star Destroyers as capital ships.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/Anaxes_Republic_Navy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200515144531)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/Anaxes_Republic_Navy.png/revision/latest?cb=20200515144531) 

The Republic Navy utilized *Venator*-class Star Destroyers as capital ships.

 

Along with the [*Acclamator*-class transgalactic military assault ship](/wiki/Acclamator-class_transgalactic_military_assault_ship "Acclamator-class transgalactic military assault ship") and other support vessels, the [*Venator*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Venator-class_Star_Destroyer "Venator-class Star Destroyer") was the mainstay [warship](/wiki/Warship "Warship") of the Republic Navy.[[141]](#cite_note-TCW_film-141) Part cargo transport and part troop carrier, the Venator was also developed for ship-to-ship combat. The Venator notably contained a large hangar for housing state-of the-art Republic starfighters.[[142]](#cite_note-VenatorDB-142)

The Republic Navy fielded various ships over the course of the war.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) Early models included the [V-19 Torrent starfighter](/wiki/V-19_Torrent_starfighter "V-19 Torrent starfighter")[[141]](#cite_note-TCW_film-141) and the [Clone Z-95 Headhunter](/wiki/Clone_Z-95_starfighter "Clone Z-95 starfighter").[[143]](#cite_note-Darkness-143) New fighters were added to the Navy in the final months of the war.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) The [Aggressive ReConnaissance-170 starfighter](/wiki/Aggressive_ReConnaissance-170_starfighter "Aggressive ReConnaissance-170 starfighter") represented the latest design in starfighter technology,[[144]](#cite_note-ARC-170-144) while the [Alpha-3 *Nimbus*-class V-wing starfighters](/wiki/Alpha-3_Nimbus-class_V-wing_starfighter "Alpha-3 Nimbus-class V-wing starfighter") incorporated the design improvements of the ARC-170 an the earlier V-19.[[145]](#cite_note-V-wing-145)

### Jedi Order[]

:   "*They have numbers on their side. And the faith of the Republic.*"  
    "*For the moment. In time, and with careful planning, they will lose both.*"
:   ―Darth Maul and Darth Sidious, on the Jedi Order[[146]](#cite_note-Age_of_Republic-146)

 [![The Jedi Order served the Galactic Republic as guardians of peace and justice.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DuelonCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111028234030) [![The Jedi Order served the Galactic Republic as guardians of peace and justice.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DuelonCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111028234030)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DuelonCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111028234030) 

The Jedi Order served the Galactic Republic as guardians of peace and justice.

 

The Galactic Republic placed its faith in and full trust into the Jedi Order,[[146]](#cite_note-Age_of_Republic-146) relying on Jedi Knights to safeguard peace and maintain justice in the realm.[[47]](#cite_note-JediDB-47) It was with the Order's aid that the Galactic Senate was able to govern the galaxy for a thousand years.[[122]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-122) The Order's allegiance was to the Senate,[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) though by the final years of the Republic, the Jedi regarded politics with skepticism, believing politicians were untrustworthy. Nonetheless, the Order maintained a close relationship with the Republic to uphold their mandate as keepers of the peace.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9)

The Order could identify Force-sensitives shortly after their birth, as long as they were born within the Republic.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10) Offering a Force-sensitive child to the Order was considered a great honor by the majority of the Republic's population, as well as a personal sacrifice.[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26) The Order became the true family of every child brought into its ranks,[[147]](#cite_note-TheGathering-147) and Jedi doctrine did not permit them to know their birth families. Therefore, familial attachment was surrendered in service to the Order.[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26)

 [![With the fall of the Jedi Order, the Galactic Republic was transformed into the Galactic Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/Burning_of_the_Temple.png/revision/latest?cb=20130207012022) [![With the fall of the Jedi Order, the Galactic Republic was transformed into the Galactic Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/Burning_of_the_Temple.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130207012022)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/Burning_of_the_Temple.png/revision/latest?cb=20130207012022) 

With the fall of the Jedi Order, the Galactic Republic was transformed into the Galactic Empire.

 

While the Order numbered ten-thousand strong at the height of the Clone Wars,[[148]](#cite_note-Siege-148) their ranks were insufficient for the defense of the Republic. Therefore, the Jedi were compelled to lead the clone army[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9) with the aim of bringing a swift and decisive end to the conflict between the Republic and the Separatists.[[84]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-84) With no end to the war in sight, however, anti-war protests broke out on Coruscant where Republic citizens decried their leaders and the Jedi alike.[[1]](#cite_note-RepublicDB-1) When the Clone Wars ended, Darth Sidious accused the Order of staging a rebellion to overthrow the Senate and their chancellor. The Senate supported the chancellor's actions, which included the purging of the Order followed by the Republic's reorganization into the Galactic Empire.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2)

## Economy[]

:   "*The Republic is near bankruptcy due to the cost of this war!*"
:   ―Bail Organa[[149]](#cite_note-HoBS-149)

The [Republic credit](/wiki/Galactic_Credit_Standard "Galactic Credit Standard") was the [currency](/wiki/Currency "Currency") of the Galactic Republic. Beyond Republic space, however, credits had no value on frontier worlds like Tatooine.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10)

The Republic possessed immense economic power,[[150]](#cite_note-CoruscantDB-150) having maintained peace—with the aid of the Jedi Knights—throughout the known galaxy for almost a millennium. Peace, in turn, promoted commerce. Under the Republic's protection, Naboo and other culturally rich worlds were able to profit from lucrative tourism.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

 [![Corporations possessed considerable influence in galactic politics during the era of the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/CardDodSaam_HoBS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130518024750) [![Corporations possessed considerable influence in galactic politics during the era of the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/CardDodSaam_HoBS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130518024750)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b6/CardDodSaam_HoBS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130518024750) 

Corporations possessed considerable influence in galactic politics during the era of the Republic.

 

The business sector experienced an exponential growth in wealth and influence through widespread commercialism, with massive corporations funneling substantial amounts of capital into advertising their essential services to the wider galaxy. This unbridled "brand-building" initiative generated steady profits for vast enterprises like the Trade Federation.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

The Republic's expansion into the Outer Rim Territories proved lucrative to both the galactic government and the private sector. [Eleven Star Marketing](/wiki/Eleven_Star_Marketing "Eleven Star Marketing"), a subsidiary of the Trade Federation, worked closely with the [Republic Ministry of Economic Development](/wiki/Republic_Ministry_of_Economic_Development "Republic Ministry of Economic Development") to [propagandize](/wiki/Settle_the_Outer_Rim "Settle the Outer Rim") the exploration and colonization of the Outer Rim, convincing the lower class citizens of the Inner Rim to see the galactic frontier as an opportunity for profit. This arrangement would entangle Republic politicians with corporate lobbyists, both of which profited from the flow of settlers who had to pay tariffs and registration fees in order to reach the Outer Rim through one of the Federation's hyperspace routes.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

 [![The Republic filled its war chest by encouraging its citizens to buy war bonds.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/80/Buy_Republic_War_Bonds.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170106125031) [![The Republic filled its war chest by encouraging its citizens to buy war bonds.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/80/Buy_Republic_War_Bonds.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20170106125031)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/80/Buy_Republic_War_Bonds.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170106125031) 

The Republic filled its war chest by encouraging its citizens to buy war bonds.

 

The Separatist Crisis had a significant impact on the Republic economy, with major worlds, like Serenno, Raxus, and Onderon seceding from the pan-galactic union. As a result, the Republic lost access to the resources and tax revenue of the Separatist worlds. Diminished taxation revenue only compounded the Republic's debt, throwing the Senate into a crisis that ultimately led to open war between the Republic and the Separatist Alliance.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

The Clone Wars disrupted the galactic economy as the Senate exhausted its options to fund the Grand Army of the Republic while staving off bankruptcy.[[149]](#cite_note-HoBS-149) The government urged its people to buy [war bonds](/wiki/War_bond "War bond"), using [propaganda](/wiki/Buy_Republic_War_Bonds "Buy Republic War Bonds") to convince the citizenry that it was their patriotic duty to give financial support to the war effort. In addition, the Republic sought to keep its war chest filled by imposing higher taxes on civilian skylanes, however unprecedented it was on cosmopolitan worlds like Coruscant.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

The Senate also weighed the need for additional clone troopers against the corresponding cost of growing supplemental units to replenish the Grand Army's ranks.[[149]](#cite_note-HoBS-149) Funding the military had all but bankrupted the Republic treasury, which, in turn, shut down some of the basic services that the Republic had always provided for civilians who lived in the lower levels of Coruscant.[[151]](#cite_note-Pursuit_of_Peace-151)

 [![The Senate voted in favor of deregulating the banks in order to continue financing the Republic war effort.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/Military_enhancement_bill.png/revision/latest?cb=20130518031752) [![The Senate voted in favor of deregulating the banks in order to continue financing the Republic war effort.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/Military_enhancement_bill.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130518031752)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/Military_enhancement_bill.png/revision/latest?cb=20130518031752) 

The Senate voted in favor of deregulating the banks in order to continue financing the Republic war effort.

 

The Republic imposed regulations on the banking industry prior to the Clone Wars, but the war's increasing cost led the Senate to consider deregulating the banks in order to access new lines of credit. After much debate, the Senate passed the [Republic financial reform bill](/wiki/Republic_financial_reform_bill "Republic financial reform bill"). The banks were deregulated, and the Republic submitted applications for further loans to support the production of more clone units.[[149]](#cite_note-HoBS-149)

Following the Republic [invasion of Scipio](/wiki/Invasion_of_Scipio "Invasion of Scipio"), the [InterGalactic Banking Clan](/wiki/InterGalactic_Banking_Clan "InterGalactic Banking Clan") surrendered its financial assets to the office of Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine. As a result, the Republic gained direct control over one of the galaxy's most influential commerce guilds.[[152]](#cite_note-IGBC-DB-152)

Though the Clone Wars had exacted a heavy toll on the Republic treasury,[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) the Republic remained a powerful economic force in the galaxy.[[150]](#cite_note-CoruscantDB-150) The Separatist Alliance, while supported by the resources of corporate barons,[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) was eventually overwhelmed by the economic and military power of the Republic.[[150]](#cite_note-CoruscantDB-150)

### Science and technology[]

:   "*You know how hard it is to find all original parts from way back in the Galactic Republic?*"
:   ―Peli Motto, to Din Djarin[[153]](#cite_note-Chapter_5-153)

The Galactic Republic invested in aesthetics and technological advancements for the starship industry. During the Republic's reign, starships were designed to be aesthetically pleasing in order to meet the customers' demand for "style and elegance" in their vessels. Craftsmanship, however, gave way to practicality as the Republic transitioned into the Galactic Empire, leading to the decline of sleek lines in favor of harsh uniformity, mass production, and sheer size.[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26)

 [![Millions of identical clones were bred to fight as soldiers of the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Youngcloneslearning.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20201003021245) [![Millions of identical clones were bred to fight as soldiers of the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Youngcloneslearning.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201003021245)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Youngcloneslearning.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20201003021245) 

Millions of identical clones were bred to fight as soldiers of the Republic.

 

Cloning was a science in which an organism was "genetically duplicated into one or more identical copies." While neither the Senate nor the Jedi had any knowledge of the clone army's development prior to the Clone Wars, the Republic became heavily invested in the field of genetics throughout its conflict with the Separatists. The Kaminoans used their skills to transform the science of cloning into big business, resulting in the mass production of clone troopers who numbered in the millions. Their expertise all but perfected the art of genetic duplication. However, cloning [humans](/wiki/Human "Human") was still a flawed science that occasionally produced aberrations. Nevertheless, the Kaminoans' cloning methods made it possible to alter clones at the genetic level, making them more docile and age twice as fast as natural-born humans.[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26) They were also just as capable of engineering a clone for the purpose of pure genetic replication, giving it neither growth acceleration nor behavioral modification for greater docility.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_II-9)

 [![The Clone Wars drove the Republic's technological advancement.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/RotS_Acclamators_depart.png/revision/latest?cb=20181207002700) [![The Clone Wars drove the Republic's technological advancement.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/RotS_Acclamators_depart.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20181207002700)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/RotS_Acclamators_depart.png/revision/latest?cb=20181207002700) 

The Clone Wars drove the Republic's technological advancement.

 

The Clone Wars gave the Republic an incentive to spearhead technological innovation in spacecraft and terrestrial transportation for military purposes. The result was a legacy with far-reaching effects in the industry of science and technology. The Star Destroyer, the most visible representative of modern military [capital ships](/wiki/Capital_ship "Capital ship"), originated with the development of the Republic Navy's *Venator*-class Star Destroyer. The [X-wing starfighter](/wiki/X-wing_starfighter "X-wing starfighter") evolved from the [Z-95 Headhunter](/wiki/Z-95_Headhunter "Z-95 Headhunter"); the [BTL Y-wing starfighter](/wiki/BTL_Y-wing_starfighter "BTL Y-wing starfighter") was developed during the Clone Wars, and was still considered relevant long after the Republic's time. The Republic developed all terrain [walkers](/wiki/Walker "Walker"), including the six-[legged](/wiki/Limb "Limb") [All Terrain Tactical Enforcer](/wiki/All_Terrain_Tactical_Enforcer "All Terrain Tactical Enforcer"), as a response to the Separatist [Armored Assault Tank](/wiki/Armored_Assault_Tank_Mk_I "Armored Assault Tank Mk I") and other droid battle tanks. This in turn influenced the developmental design of far larger vehicles, such as the Imperial [All Terrain Armored Transport](/wiki/All_Terrain_Armored_Transport "All Terrain Armored Transport") and the First Order [All Terrain MegaCaliber Six](/wiki/All_Terrain_MegaCaliber_Six "All Terrain MegaCaliber Six"), than what the Republic fielded in the Clone Wars.[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26)

 [![The electro-proton bomb was capable of destroying an army of droids in a single attack.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Electro-proton_explosion.png/revision/latest?cb=20120911234804) [![The electro-proton bomb was capable of destroying an army of droids in a single attack.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Electro-proton_explosion.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120911234804)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/Electro-proton_explosion.png/revision/latest?cb=20120911234804) 

The electro-proton bomb was capable of destroying an army of droids in a single attack.

 

The Republic employed brilliant [scientists](/wiki/Scientist "Scientist"), such as [Doctor](/wiki/Doctor "Doctor") [Sionver Boll](/wiki/Sionver_Boll "Sionver Boll")[[154]](#cite_note-Sionver_Boll_DB-154) and Doctor [Nala Se](/wiki/Nala_Se "Nala Se"),[[155]](#cite_note-Nala_Se_DB-155) who contributed their expertise to the war effort against the Separatists.[[90]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-90)[[156]](#cite_note-Conspiracy-156) Boll developed the electro-proton bomb,[[154]](#cite_note-Sionver_Boll_DB-154) an experimental explosive device capable of generating a massive burst of [electromagnetic pulse](/wiki/Electromagnetic_pulse "Electromagnetic pulse") energy to disable battle droids and any other form of technology.[[90]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-90) Nala Se was the foremost scientist in the field of cloning; she supervised the development of the Republic's clone army,[[155]](#cite_note-Nala_Se_DB-155) although Boll was also familiar with cloning as Chancellor Palpatine ordered her to clone a dead Zillo Beast.[[94]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast_Strikes_Back-94)

 [![The Death Star originated from the Republic Special Weapons Group and the Separatist schematics for the Ultimate Weapon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c6/UltimateWeaponPlans-AOTC.png/revision/latest?cb=20250127022332) [![The Death Star originated from the Republic Special Weapons Group and the Separatist schematics for the Ultimate Weapon.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c6/UltimateWeaponPlans-AOTC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250127022332)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c6/UltimateWeaponPlans-AOTC.png/revision/latest?cb=20250127022332) 

The Death Star originated from the Republic Special Weapons Group and the Separatist schematics for the Ultimate Weapon.

 

The [Republic Special Weapons Group](/wiki/Republic_Special_Weapons_Group "Republic Special Weapons Group") was formed to oversee the development of military technology more advanced than conventional weapons of warfare.[[157]](#cite_note-Rogue_One:_Rebel_Dossier-157) The group was composed of technologists like Wilhuff Tarkin and [Orson Callan Krennic](/wiki/Orson_Callan_Krennic "Orson Callan Krennic");[[7]](#cite_note-Catalyst-7) using the [Geonosians](/wiki/Geonosian "Geonosian")' [schematics](/wiki/Death_Star_plans "Death Star plans") for a [moon](/wiki/Moon "Moon")-sized [battle station](/wiki/Battle_station "Battle station"), they began implementing plans to construct the [ultimate weapon](/wiki/Death_Star "Death Star"). Their work continued after the Republic fell, and after years of delay the [DS-1 Death Star Mobile Battle Station](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station") was made operational by the Empire. Both its size and power inspired the creation of more advanced weapons with the [capacity to destroy planets](/wiki/Superlaser "Superlaser"), from the Imperial [DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station](/wiki/DS-2_Death_Star_II_Mobile_Battle_Station "DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station") to the First Order's [Starkiller Base](/wiki/Starkiller_Base "Starkiller Base") and the [axial superlaser](/wiki/Axial_superlaser "Axial superlaser") [cannons](/wiki/Cannon "Cannon") of the [Final Order](/wiki/Final_Order "Final Order")'s [*Xyston*-class Star Destroyers](/wiki/Xyston-class_Star_Destroyer "Xyston-class Star Destroyer").[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26)

According to [Peli Motto](/wiki/Peli_Motto "Peli Motto"), a [technician](/wiki/Technician "Technician") who lived on Tatooine, technology from the era of the Galactic Republic was rare by the time of the New Republic Era. Nevertheless, Motto endeavored to acquire the parts needed to [rebuild](/wiki/Din_Djarin%27s_N-1_starfighter "Din Djarin's N-1 starfighter") a derelict [N-1 starfighter](/wiki/N-1_starfighter "N-1 starfighter") for her client, the Mandalorian [Din Djarin](/wiki/Din_Djarin "Din Djarin"). As a Galactic Republic-era starfighter, the N-1 was made of pre-Empire handmade components and therefore not manufactured by droids. One such component was a [turbonic venturi power assimilator](/wiki/Turbonic_venturi_power_assimilator "Turbonic venturi power assimilator") that Motto acquired from a group of [Jawas](/wiki/Jawa "Jawa").[[153]](#cite_note-Chapter_5-153)

## Society and culture[]

### Civilization[]

:   "*Tales of its founding have been occluded by the haze of intervening millennia, and its rebirth a thousand years ago was regarded as the latest evolution in an unending cycle. Like the greatest of trees, however, the Republic's decline began from within, with a deep rot that was not apparent until it was too late.*"
:   ―Janyor[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

 [![The Core Worlds represented the wealthiest and most prestigious region in the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/Coruscant_landscape_RotS.png/revision/latest?cb=20140825132625) [![The Core Worlds represented the wealthiest and most prestigious region in the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/Coruscant_landscape_RotS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140825132625)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/Coruscant_landscape_RotS.png/revision/latest?cb=20140825132625) 

The Core Worlds represented the wealthiest and most prestigious region in the Galactic Republic.

 

The Galactic Republic governed the galaxy as a democratic union,[[1]](#cite_note-RepublicDB-1) and as such, it featured a diverse society of humans and various alien [species](/wiki/Species "Species").[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) Coruscant in particular was emblematic of Republic society with its diverse mix of citizens and culture, making the Republic capital the "vibrant heart" of the galaxy.[[150]](#cite_note-CoruscantDB-150) Overall, being a galactic government, trillions lived under the Republic, with every one of those beings an individual who had their own thoughts and opinions on current issues; as such, complete consensus was impossible, yet successful Chancellors, like Lina Soh, nonetheless proved it was possible to bring about effective, galactic rule. In Soh's case, she argued to her people the advantage of coming together to make life better for all. Others failed to bring about that same unity by making impossible promises, threats, or abusing power.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

The Core Worlds, where Coruscant was located, was home to the most developed systems in the Republic. Various Core planets served as capitals for galactic governments such as the Old Republic, the Empire, and the New Republic. The prosperity of the Core made its worlds the wealthiest and most prestigious members of the Republic, though it was also a source of tension between the Core and the more distant regions of the galaxy. People who lived outside of the Core generally viewed "Core Worlders" as arrogant, entitled, and apathetic to the well-being and needs of other regions. A common criticism of Republic politics was that the system disproportionately favored the Core Worlds to the point of ignoring the rest of the galaxy.[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26)

 [![The Republic capital's lower levels were ridden with crime and poverty.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/Level_1313_DB.png/revision/latest?cb=20160320192313) [![The Republic capital's lower levels were ridden with crime and poverty.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/Level_1313_DB.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160320192313)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/Level_1313_DB.png/revision/latest?cb=20160320192313) 

The Republic capital's lower levels were ridden with crime and poverty.

 

Coruscant was perceived as perpetuating the Core Worlds' reputation for extreme wealth and privilege. Notwithstanding its unique status as the galactic capital, the whole planet was covered by a city of levels built upon levels throughout the ages of galactic history. The tallest skyscrapers rose over five-thousand levels above the planet's natural surface, and only those who could afford to live in the upper city had access to the comfortable and luxurious lifestyle for which Coruscant was famous. The disparity was such that the lower levels were notorious for widespread crime, poverty, and being devoid of natural sunlight.[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26)

Republic architecture was an architectural style that demonstrated sweeping lines. This particular design was prominently featured on the city-covered planet of Coruscant, although by the time of the Clone Wars, the Republic gradually adopted a brutalist or bold form of architecture. Introduced by military architects such as Orson Krennic, it ultimately supplanted the Republic style as the dominant architectural form of the Galactic Empire.[[158]](#cite_note-Visual_Guide-158)

[Galactic Basic Standard](/wiki/Galactic_Basic_Standard "Galactic Basic Standard") was the most prevalent [language](/wiki/Language "Language") in the Republic,[[159]](#cite_note-Aliens_of_the_Galaxy-159) spoken primarily by humans[[160]](#cite_note-sweWI-160) and the [Pantorans](/wiki/Pantoran "Pantoran").[[161]](#cite_note-sweTA-161) A heavily accented dialect of Basic, with many differences in grammar and vocabulary, was spoken by the Gungans of Naboo.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10) The translation of the Sith language, known as [ur-Kittât](/wiki/Ur-Kitt%C3%A2t "Ur-Kittât"), was forbidden under Galactic Republic law. [Protocol droids](/wiki/Protocol_droid "Protocol droid") were consequently programmed against translating the language of the Sith. Darth Sidious believed that the Republic outlawed ur-Kittât out of fear of the Sith Order and its knowledge.[[162]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-162)

 [![Republic citizens turned away from galactic politics to follow escapist pursuits.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0a/GalaxiesOperaHouse.png/revision/latest?cb=20130202025152) [![Republic citizens turned away from galactic politics to follow escapist pursuits.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0a/GalaxiesOperaHouse.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130202025152)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0a/GalaxiesOperaHouse.png/revision/latest?cb=20130202025152) 

Republic citizens turned away from galactic politics to follow escapist pursuits.

 

The peaceful age of the Republic allowed the people of the galaxy to pursue leisure activities, some of which achieved galactic-level attention. The [Boonta Eve Classic](/wiki/Boonta_Eve_Classic "Boonta Eve Classic"), while based on the independent Outer Rim world of Tatooine, beyond the Republic frontier, received coverage and attention as far as the Core Worlds. Prior to the Clone Wars, the Republic's twilight years became an era of escapism as citizens of all classes sought entertaining distractions from their daily lives. Professional podrace circuits and other circuses diverted the people's attention from the growing corruption that permeated the Galactic Senate. Nevertheless, the general public's fascination with various forms of entertainment was driven by an innate desire for stories about good versus evil and situations of escalating danger.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

 [![The Jedi Order eschewed prestige and celebrity, making them mysterious to the Republic they served.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9f/JediTemple_cloudysky.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140802205911) [![The Jedi Order eschewed prestige and celebrity, making them mysterious to the Republic they served.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9f/JediTemple_cloudysky.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140802205911)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9f/JediTemple_cloudysky.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140802205911) 

The Jedi Order eschewed prestige and celebrity, making them mysterious to the Republic they served.

 

Whereas the Republic evolved through the centuries of its existence, the Jedi Order remained rooted in its ancient traditions, effectively putting the [Jedi Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code") at odds with a galactic society that strongly favored the future over the past. The inhabitants of the Core Worlds became fixated on notions of fame and fashion, and had little interest in Jedi principles like faith and tradition. The Order maintained its place in the Republic by relying on historic precedent, serving as keepers of peace and justice. Unlike corporate institutions that marketed their services to the greater galaxy, the Order had little desire to promote itself through image-building. Aside from those who witnessed the Jedi's heroics[[163]](#cite_note-Tipping_Points-163) and were awed by their [Force powers](/wiki/Force_power "Force power"), the Order and its ways were forever mysterious to the majority of the Republic citizenry. The Jedi were seen by the public as an order of mystics at best and, at worst, regarded as a zealous sect of warmongers.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

 [![A variant of the Republic crest was used during the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/Republic6SpokedBenduSymbol-RotS.svg/revision/latest?cb=20080311202138) [![A variant of the Republic crest was used during the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/Republic6SpokedBenduSymbol-RotS.svg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20080311202138)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/Republic6SpokedBenduSymbol-RotS.svg/revision/latest?cb=20080311202138) 

A variant of the Republic crest was used during the Clone Wars.

 

As a result of territorial expansion, the Republic developed a sense of manifest destiny. This cultural belief was cultivated by Republic propagandists who sought to foster civic pride among the populace so that they would ultimately feel duty-bound to support the Republic's expansion from rim to rim. There was an exponential growth in Republic patriotism due to the Clone Wars and the accompanying propaganda that promoted loyalty to the state. Patriotic messages stirred an entire generation into action; however, they could not enlist in the Grand Army as its ranks were exclusive to clone troopers. Nevertheless, Republic citizens felt obliged to do their part by purchasing war bonds, reporting acts of treason, and making sacrifices to support the war effort.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) The [Republic crest](/wiki/Republic_crest "Republic crest"), the symbol of a united galaxy under the Force,[[164]](#cite_note-Complete_Vehicles_2018-164) was emblazoned on military war machines and heraldry, featuring more prominently than before.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

Although the Republic expanded into the Outer Rim Territories, the region was too underdeveloped to have the same stability as the Core Worlds. As the galaxy's largest region, the Outer Rim featured a myriad of diversity through its various planets and species. The Republic government had little oversight over the Outer Rim due to the region's distance from the Core, and as such the Outer Rim remained known for its lawless, sparsely populated, and primitive worlds. Republic law was virtually non-existent in the Outer Rim; as a result, bounty hunters, outlaws and smugglers were able to operate with impunity,[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26) and [slavery](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery") was still practiced in spite of the Republic's anti-slave laws.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10)

### Xenophobia[]

:   "*Under Gunray's tenure, the Trade Federation would loudly counter such claims as common anti-Neimoidian prejudice.*"
:   ―Janyor[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

 [![A popular stereotype of the Neimoidian race was the fat plutocrat who embodied greed and treachery.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/Taxation_Without_Federation-SW_Propaganda.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170305031011) [![A popular stereotype of the Neimoidian race was the fat plutocrat who embodied greed and treachery.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/Taxation_Without_Federation-SW_Propaganda.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20170305031011)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/Taxation_Without_Federation-SW_Propaganda.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170305031011) 

A popular stereotype of the Neimoidian race was the fat plutocrat who embodied greed and treachery.

 

During the High Republic Era, Chancellor Soh wanted to promote unity amongst the various species that made up the Republic, using the phrase "We are all the Republic" to let the population know they were all part of the system;[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6) however, [xenophobia](/wiki/Xenophobia "Xenophobia") was an issue in a society as diverse as the Republic. Although the Republic officially promoted unity among its member worlds[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) and outlawed the enslavement of [sentient](/wiki/Sentience "Sentience") species,[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10) some people were subjected to racial stereotypes. [Neimoidians](/wiki/Neimoidian "Neimoidian"), for example, were considered obese, duplicitous and avaricious by some, including those who harbored anti-corporate views. This perception of their race was a product of Neimoidian culture, which cultivated a "survival of the fittest" mentality in Neimoidian [younglings](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling").[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

The Trade Federation used xenophobic sentiments as a means to silence its critics, insinuating that those who sought to [curtail the Federation's massive influence](/wiki/Taxation_Without_Federation "Taxation Without Federation") were prejudiced towards its Neimoidian leaders. The [Muuns](/wiki/Muun "Muun") likewise had an image problem due to their monopoly in the InterGalactic Banking Clan. In general Muuns saw little need to build a relationship of stability and trust with the galaxy; they simply assumed that their place in society was to continue dominating galactic finances. Their cultural standards informed their business practices; therefore, Muun-sponsored advertisements were viewed as "distant and disconnected."[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

During the Clone Wars, anti-alien prejudice grew as a result of the non-human races that constituted the Confederacy of Independent Systems. Vice Chancellor Mas Amedda sought to promote the Republic's multicultural aspect, having taken notice of the attention given to human citizens by the Republic media. Rather than reporting on Amedda's effort to showcase Republic diversity, [HoloNet News](/wiki/HoloNet_News "HoloNet News") outlets focused on the Vice Chancellor's self-inclusion as the sole [Chagrian](/wiki/Chagrian "Chagrian") in an assembly of various aliens. The populace decried Amedda's [message of strength and unity](/wiki/Strength_and_Unity "Strength and Unity"), and considered him an egocentric narcissist.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

 [![The Clone Wars fueled the Republic population's anti-droid sentiment.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/Keep_Our_Republic_Secure.png/revision/latest?cb=20201011180124) [![The Clone Wars fueled the Republic population's anti-droid sentiment.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/Keep_Our_Republic_Secure.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20201011180124)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/Keep_Our_Republic_Secure.png/revision/latest?cb=20201011180124) 

The Clone Wars fueled the Republic population's anti-droid sentiment.

 

The Clone Wars also inflamed the population's [anti-droid sentiment](/wiki/Anti-droid_sentiment "Anti-droid sentiment") to new levels due in no small part to the Separatists' reliance on battle droids. Droids had long become commonplace in galactic society, and though machines had always been the property of organics, the war cemented the view that droids were an existential threat to biological life. The Republic capitalized on this sentiment, using propaganda to illustrate droids as ruthless and dangerous tools of destruction. While the the concept of "droid terror" was embodied by battlefield machines, such as the [B1-series battle droid](/wiki/B1-series_battle_droid "B1-series battle droid"), [B2-series super battle droid](/wiki/B2-series_super_battle_droid "B2-series super battle droid"), and the [droideka](/wiki/Droideka "Droideka"), administrative [aide](/wiki/Aide "Aide") droids were viewed as a different kind of "droid threat" to Republic security. There was a growing fear among the Core's affluent population that the personal assistant droids of businessbeings and government administrators could be co-opted through spyware and used for Separatist [espionage](/wiki/Spy "Spy").[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

Despite the Jedi Order's millennia of service to the Republic,[[26]](#cite_note-TSWB-26) there was widespread [anti-Jedi sentiment](/wiki/Anti-Jedi_sentiment "Anti-Jedi sentiment") as a result of the Clone Wars.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) The Sith plotted to undermine the relationship between the Republic citizenry and their Jedi guardians,[[146]](#cite_note-Age_of_Republic-146) using the Clone Wars to shake the Republic's faith in the Order.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) The Order fought hard to bring a swift and decisive end to the conflict,[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) but many citizens believed that the Jedi were warmongers. This perception was able to grow due in part to the Jedi's reluctance to accept accolades or embrace the fame of their status. It was the Order's preference to serve but not engage the populace; as such, the population's anti-Jedi views were the result of the Order's cultural absence as opposed to an actual refutation of their ways.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

## Astrography[]

:   "*Republic wordsmiths and artists collaborated to create a sense of civic duty, of manifest destiny, and of deep obligation to spread the Republic banner from Rim to Rim.*"
:   ―Janyor[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

 [![Coruscant, the capital of the Republic, was located in the heart of the Core Worlds.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Coruscant_system-TPM.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200924030624) [![Coruscant, the capital of the Republic, was located in the heart of the Core Worlds.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Coruscant_system-TPM.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200924030624)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Coruscant_system-TPM.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200924030624) 

Coruscant, the capital of the Republic, was located in the heart of the Core Worlds.

 

With Coruscant—birthplace of the human species[[165]](#cite_note-Uprising-165)—as its capital,[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) the expansion of the Galactic Republic occurred along pioneering [hyperspace routes](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route"). Survey teams established navigational beacons in outlying territories such as the [Tertiary Usaita system](/wiki/Tertiary_Usaita_system "Tertiary Usaita system"),[[166]](#cite_note-Weapon_of_a_Jedi-166) allowing colonists from the Core Worlds to venture outward towards the Outer Rim in search of opportunity and a better life.[[167]](#cite_note-Smuggler's_Run-167)

The Galactic Republic existed across the known galaxy, stretching from the Core Worlds to the Outer Rim Territories. The Core Worlds was the heartland of the Republic, home to cosmopolitan worlds such as Coruscant[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) and [Hosnian Prime](/wiki/Hosnian_Prime "Hosnian Prime")[[168]](#cite_note-Hosnian_Prime_DB-168) as well as Alderaan, one of the oldest and most prestigious planets in the Republic.[[169]](#cite_note-Alderaan_DB-169) Over time, Republic expansionism led to the annexation of new member worlds.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) The planet Naboo, located in the Mid Rim, was annexed by the Republic[[91]](#cite_note-Crisis_on_Naboo-91) in [867 BBY](/wiki/867_BBY "867 BBY").[[170]](#cite_note-Crisis_date-170)

 [![The Galactic Republic was a democratic union that spanned across the known galaxy for a thousand years.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/The_Galaxy_-_TROS_Visual_Dictionary.png/revision/latest?cb=20250802011341) [![The Galactic Republic was a democratic union that spanned across the known galaxy for a thousand years.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/The_Galaxy_-_TROS_Visual_Dictionary.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250802011341)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/The_Galaxy_-_TROS_Visual_Dictionary.png/revision/latest?cb=20250802011341) 

The Galactic Republic was a democratic union that spanned across the known galaxy for a thousand years.

 

During the High Republic Era, during which time the Republic actively sought out new hyperspace lanes[[63]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-63) and new member worlds in the Outer Rim,[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6) Chancellor Orlen Mollo reflected on the positive paradox that was Republic expansion; with each new hyperlane, the Republic grew while the galactic community became smaller. As such, it was easier for the galaxy's planets to interact with each other. Beyond prospecting new hyperspace routes, the Republic was also actively working to expand communications[[63]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-63) into a functioning network in the Rim,[[57]](#cite_note-Blade_1-57) attempting to further alliances, and hoping to shut down brewing conflicts.[[63]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-63) The Republic exerted most of its power from the Core Worlds to the borders of the Mid Rim, to the extent that corporations conducted their legally dubious practices in regions where the Republic held little sway[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) despite the work done to bring those worlds into the galactic community during the High Republic Era.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

 [![The Republic's colonization of the Outer Rim Territories was motivated by overpopulation, poverty, and a sense of manifest destiny.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/Settle_the_Outer_Rim.png/revision/latest?cb=20170305031631) [![The Republic's colonization of the Outer Rim Territories was motivated by overpopulation, poverty, and a sense of manifest destiny.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/Settle_the_Outer_Rim.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170305031631)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/Settle_the_Outer_Rim.png/revision/latest?cb=20170305031631) 

The Republic's colonization of the Outer Rim Territories was motivated by overpopulation, poverty, and a sense of manifest destiny.

 

Faced with issues like overpopulation and poverty among the lower classes, the Republic turned its attention to the Outer Rim, adopting a policy of expansion toward the uncharted territories of the known galaxy's farthest frontier. Those who inhabited the congested worlds of the galactic core were beckoned into deep space by political and corporate sponsored messages of life filled with adventure and mystery.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) Such a call to new horizons could be seen during the High Republic Era, where brave citizens and families of the overpopulated Core and Colonies worlds moved to the Outer Rim through the few well-mapped hyperspace routes into the Rim. Still, the Outer Rim in specific could be home to dangers like the Nihil who took advantage of the lack of Republic law, with the Nihil waging war with the Republic for daring to enter their homelands.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6) Into the late Republic Era, the Outer Rim remained a region where the Republic held little authority[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10) despite the work done in the High Republic period.[[6]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-6)

 [![The Republic's dominion extended beyond the boundaries of the galaxy, reaching as far as the extragalactic world of Kamino.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/KaminoBlockade-ARCT.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111229200031) [![The Republic's dominion extended beyond the boundaries of the galaxy, reaching as far as the extragalactic world of Kamino.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/KaminoBlockade-ARCT.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111229200031)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/KaminoBlockade-ARCT.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111229200031) 

The Republic's dominion extended beyond the boundaries of the galaxy, reaching as far as the extragalactic world of Kamino.

 

Although the Republic opposed secession, it effectively lost control over the territories that formed the Separatist Alliance. Its territorial extent changed numerous times over the course of the Clone Wars, with worlds lost and reclaimed by the Grand Army of the Republic. However, the Republic also gained new territory as a result of the war. Geonosis, the planet where the Separatist Droid Army was secretly constructed, existed beyond the Republic's borders.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16) The Republic Military [occupied](/wiki/Occupation_of_Geonosis "Occupation of Geonosis") the [Geonosian](/wiki/Geonosian "Geonosian") homeworld after the First Battle of Geonosis, and subsequently returned to [reconquer](/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Geonosis "Second Battle of Geonosis") the planet after it fell back under Separatist control.[[8]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Separatists-8) The [Kaminoan government](/wiki/Ruling_Council_(Kamino) "Ruling Council (Kamino)") formally joined the Republic; as such, Kamino[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)—an [extragalactic](/wiki/Extragalactic "Extragalactic") planet[[85]](#cite_note-SW:CL-85)—was accorded full representation in the Galactic Senate, having supplied the Republic with its clone industry.[[16]](#cite_note-SWP-16)

## Behind the scenes[]

The Galactic Republic was first mentioned in the new *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* [canon](/wiki/Canon "Canon") as the "Old Republic" through the [1977](/wiki/1977 "1977") film [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"), directed by [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas").[[19]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-19) The entity first appeared and was first identified as the "Galactic Republic" in the [1999](/wiki/1999 "1999") film [*Star Wars*: Episode I *The Phantom Menace*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace "Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace"), also directed by Lucas.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_I-10)

[↑](#cite_ref-New_Republic_date_17-0) The *[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker:_The_Visual_Dictionary "Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary")* dates the formation of the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic") to thirty [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the [Starkiller Incident](/wiki/Hosnian_Cataclysm "Hosnian Cataclysm"), which *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* dates to [34 ABY](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY"). Therefore, the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic") must have been formed in [4 ABY](/wiki/4_ABY "4 ABY"). 18. ↑ [18.0](#cite_ref-Aftermath_18-0) [18.1](#cite_ref-Aftermath_18-1) [18.2](#cite_ref-Aftermath_18-2) [18.3](#cite_ref-Aftermath_18-3) [18.4](#cite_ref-Aftermath_18-4) [*Aftermath*](/wiki/Aftermath_(novel) "Aftermath (novel)") 19. ↑ [19.0](#cite_ref-Episode_IV_19-0) [19.1](#cite_ref-Episode_IV_19-1) [19.2](#cite_ref-Episode_IV_19-2) [19.3](#cite_ref-Episode_IV_19-3) [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope") 20. [↑](#cite_ref-Blood_Court_note_22-0) *[Unlimited Power](/wiki/Unlimited_Power "Unlimited Power")* states that the [Blood Court's](/wiki/Blood_Monarch "Blood Monarch") hereditary line dated 20,000 [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") prior to the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era") when it joined the Galactic Republic in its early formation. 23. ↑ [23.0](#cite_ref-Chaos_Rising_23-0) [23.1](#cite_ref-Chaos_Rising_23-1) [23.2](#cite_ref-Chaos_Rising_23-2) *[Thrawn Ascendancy: Chaos Rising](/wiki/Thrawn_Ascendancy:_Chaos_Rising "Thrawn Ascendancy: Chaos Rising")* 24. [↑](#cite_ref-Capital_24-0) According to *[Star Wars: The Force Awakens: The Visual Dictionary](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens:_The_Visual_Dictionary "Star Wars: The Force Awakens: The Visual Dictionary")*, [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant") had been the [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") of [galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") [politics](/wiki/Politics "Politics") for [millennia](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium"). However, it is stated in [*Star Wars*: Episode II *Attack of the Clones*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones") that the modern Galactic Republic, whose capital was Coruscant, was only founded about 1,000 [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"). This implies that Coruscant was also the capital of the old Galactic Republic, which the televised episode "[The Mandalore Plot](/wiki/The_Mandalore_Plot "The Mandalore Plot")" referred to as the Old Republic. 25. [↑](#cite_ref-Alderaan_DB_169-0) [StarWars-DatabankII](/wiki/Databank_(2014-) "Databank (2014-)") [Alderaan](https://www.starwars.com/databank/alderaan) in the [Databank](/wiki/Databank_(2014-) "Databank (2014-)") ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20220805133918/https://www.starwars.com/databank/alderaan)) 170. [↑](#cite_ref-Crisis_date_170-0) In the TV episode "[Crisis on Naboo](/wiki/Crisis_on_Naboo "Crisis on Naboo")," [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") was kidnapped by [Cad Bane](/wiki/Cad_Bane "Cad Bane") "eight-hundred and forty-seven [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") [after] [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo") joined the Republic." According to *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")*, the kidnapping took place in [20 BBY](/wiki/20_BBY "20 BBY"). This places Naboo joining the Republic in [867 BBY](/wiki/867_BBY "867 BBY"). |
